# Skyrim:Special Delivery (Sylgja)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

.jpg)

Sylgja needs a delivery made.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Sylgja](/wiki/Skyrim:Sylgja "Skyrim:Sylgja") in [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone").
2. Travel to [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing").
3. Talk to her father, [Verner](/wiki/Skyrim:Verner_Rock-Chucker "Skyrim:Verner Rock-Chucker").
4. Return to Sylgja to receive your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

_02.jpg)

Sylgja's parents work in the mine.

### Shor's Stone

In [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") you will come across [Sylgja](/wiki/Skyrim:Sylgja "Skyrim:Sylgja"), who tells you that her parents live in [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") and asks if you will deliver a satchel of letters to her father there. She would take them herself, but she recently suffered a leg injury in [the local mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Redbelly_Mine "Skyrim:Redbelly Mine"). Agree to deliver the letters for her, and she gives you [her satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Sylgja%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Sylgja's Satchel").

### Darkwater Crossing

Travel to Darkwater Crossing and find Sylgja's father, [Verner Rock-Chucker](/wiki/Skyrim:Verner_Rock-Chucker "Skyrim:Verner Rock-Chucker"), who will usually be hard at work in [Goldenrock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenrock_Mine "Skyrim:Goldenrock Mine") or resting in his house nearby. Verner is pleased with the letters and asks you to deliver a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Verner%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Verner's Satchel") in return, and suggests that Sylgia will be happy to compensate you for your efforts.

### Back to Shor's Stone

Return to Shor's Stone and give Sylgja the satchel from her father. Thanking you for your efforts, she rewards you with a random piece of jewelry.

## Notes

- After completing this quest you will be able to marry Sylgja.
- This quest are marked a suggested level 1+, like a [Truth Ore Consequences](/wiki/Skyrim:Truth_Ore_Consequences "Skyrim:Truth Ore Consequences"), [Sleeping Tree Cave (Quest)](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Cave_(quest) "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Cave (quest)"), and [The Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard").

## Quest Stages

| Special Delivery (FreeformShorsStone02) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Deliver the satchel to Verner in Darkwater Crossing |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Return to Sylgja |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 200, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformShorsStone02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformShorsStone02`.

# Skyrim:Spells

## Overview

Dozens of **spells** are available for magically-inclined characters in Skyrim. Most spells (other than starting spells) are learned by reading **Spell Tomes**.

## Master Level Spells

Master-level spells are different from lower-level spells:

- They always require both hands.
- They take 3 seconds to complete.
- You cannot move while casting.
- They may be interrupted by stagger attack.

Other than the Alteration spell Dragonhide and the Restoration spell Guardian Circle, master-level spells do not benefit from dual casting perks.

When in combat, master-level spells are tricky to use because of the time required to cast them. Furthermore while casting them, you are completely vulnerable and can be interrupted by any sort of attack. Some ways around this weakness are:

- staggering your enemy first with a dual-cast spell. [Ice Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Storm "Skyrim:Ice Storm") can stagger multiple enemies at once.
- combining them with shouts such as [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") or [Ice Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Form "Skyrim:Ice Form").
- combining them with illusion and alteration crowd control effects, such as [Pacify](/wiki/Skyrim:Pacify_(spell) "Skyrim:Pacify (spell)").
- using followers or conjurations as distractions.
- combining them with high level flesh spells.
- casting them from sneak.

## Spell Notes

- The **base cost** for spells is the amount of [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") that would be necessary to cast the spell at **0 skill** without any perks. The magicka cost at 100 skill is 41% less than the base cost; the cost can also be reduced via enchanted apparel and by unlocking various perks. See [Spell Cost](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Overview#Spell_Cost "Skyrim:Magic Overview") for the full magicka cost equation.
- Skill level indicates which skill perk needs to be unlocked to decrease the spell's magicka cost. "N/A" is used for special spells whose cost is not affected by any perks.
- You will always know the spells [Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames") and [Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") by the time you start [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound"), regardless of your race, and depending on your race, other spells will also be known:
  - [Altmer](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") will also know [Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Fury "Skyrim:Fury").
  - [Bretons](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") will also know [Conjure Familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Familiar "Skyrim:Conjure Familiar").
  - [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") will also know [Sparks](/wiki/Skyrim:Sparks "Skyrim:Sparks").
- [Altmer](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") start the game with 50 extra magicka and can use [Highborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Highborn "Skyrim:Highborn") to generate magicka quickly.
- If you lack the required magicka amount to cast a spell, a "You don't have enough magicka" message will appear on the screen.
- The "Where to Get" column only lists *guaranteed* locations for obtaining the spell tomes. Most spell tomes are also available in random loot; see [Spell Tome Locations](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells#Spell_Tome_Locations "Skyrim:Spells") and the table below for details.
- For higher-level spell tomes to become available for purchase, your skill in the school must be high enough (see the table below). Also, master-level spell tomes can only be acquired once that school's ritual spell [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction)#Master_Skill_Quests "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") has been completed.
- All spell tomes have a weight of 1.
- Skill XP can be modified by scripts and by the game engine itself under various circumstances. The exact XP you receive may vary from the numbers listed here.
- Magicka cost and skill XP are rounded down, both in game and on this page. Because of this, you may find that you cannot cast a spell even though it appears you have exactly enough magicka to do so.

Tomes by Level

| Spell Level | Skill Level | Character Level, Boss Chest | Character Level, Random Chest |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Novice | 0 | 1 | 1 |
| Apprentice | 0 | 11 | 10 |
| Adept | 40 | 23 | - |
| Expert | 65 | 35 | - |
| Master | 0/90[†](#intnote_masterleveltome) | - | - |

[†](#note_masterleveltome)Master level spell tomes require the appropriate ritual spell quest to be completed to be sold; while the quests have a skill level requirement of 90 to initiate, if you have completed the quest and reset the skill by making it legendary, the spell tome should still be available for sale.

## Spell Tome Locations

Most spell tomes can be purchased from [merchants](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Skyrim:Merchants"). Novice- and apprentice-level spell tomes can be purchased from the court wizards found in each of Skyrim's cities. Higher-level spell tomes are more difficult to find: Each court wizard only stocks the adept-level spells for one school ([Farengar](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire"), [Madena](/wiki/Skyrim:Madena "Skyrim:Madena") and [Wuunferth](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuunferth_the_Unliving "Skyrim:Wuunferth the Unliving") for [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction"), [Falion](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion "Skyrim:Falion") and [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo") for [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration"), [Sybille Stentor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor") for [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") and [Wylandriah](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah "Skyrim:Wylandriah") for [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration")) and the expert-level spells can only be purchased from the specialist mages in the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). Also, adept- and expert-level spell tomes only appear in the mage's merchandise when your magic skill is high enough (40 for Adept and 65 for Expert spells). After reaching the required skill level, you must wait for the mage's merchandise to be reset (typically two days in-game), or, save, then attack the merchant and reload, before the new tomes will appear. Master-level spell tomes can only be acquired once that school's ritual spell [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction)#Quests "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") has been completed.

Nearly all spell tomes can also be found randomly as loot. The only spell tomes that can *not* be found randomly are quest-specific spell tomes (those that can not be purchased), tomes added by [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") or [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), and master-level tomes. The appearance of random tomes is dependent upon your character's overall level (but is not related to your skill in the magic school, unlike tome purchases):

- Novice: level 1+
- Apprentice: level 11+
- Adept: level 23+
- Expert: level 35+

Those random loot tomes may be found in boss chests and safes. With the [Merchant perk](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_(perk) "Skyrim:Merchant (perk)") unlocked, there is a small chance that tomes are sold by [blacksmiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Skyrim:Blacksmith"). With the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") add-on installed, tomes can also be purchased from [Morven Stroud](/wiki/Skyrim:Morven_Stroud "Skyrim:Morven Stroud").

Additionally several chests may contain low level tomes dependent on character level. Those may be carried by several spellcasters too:

- Novice: level 1+
- Apprentice: level 10+

## Bugs

- The loot list for expert level spell tomes in dungeons incorrectly uses a global variable setting that's intended to be used on vendor inventories.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.5, fixes this bug.

The overturned cart

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read *[Bounty: Lost Wares](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Lost_Wares "Skyrim:Bounty: Lost Wares")*
2. Travel to [Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn")
3. Fish for the [Aged Flin](/wiki/Skyrim:Aged_Flin "Skyrim:Aged Flin")
4. Return the bottles to [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad")

## Detailed Walkthrough

The fishing spot

This quest can be started after [Private Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:Private_Lessons "Skyrim:Private Lessons") has been completed by talking to Viriya:

:   **Know of anyone in need of fishing work around Skyrim?**
:   *"Of course. It's all in this note."*

She will then hand you a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Lost_Wares "Skyrim:Bounty: Lost Wares"), which explains that a Khajiit merchant named [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad") lost some bottles of [Aged Flin](/wiki/Skyrim:Aged_Flin "Skyrim:Aged Flin") in the river west of [Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn") and needs help retrieving them.

You will need to travel to Old Hroldan Inn and head west toward the river. When you arrive at the overturned cart, you will have to fish for three bottles of the Aged Flin.

Once you have all three bottles, travel to Ri'saad and then speak to him:

:   **Here's all of the bottles of aged flin you lost in the river.**
:   *"Excellent. And now, please accept this token of appreciation."*

He will then reward you with the [Ring of Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Khajiit "Skyrim:Ring of Khajiit").

## Notes

- There is a [hide helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Helmet "Skyrim:Hide Helmet") directly to the left of the fishing spot among some crates.

## Quest Stages

| Spirits Away (ccBGSSSE001\_Misc\_Khajiit) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 0 |  | Ri'saad, the Khajiit caravan merchant, has accidentally lost several bottles of expensive flin. He has already sold the bottles to an impatient buyer and needs to retrieve them as soon as possible. Ri'saad has put out a bounty to anyone who might be able to retrieve them from the river west of Old Hroldan Inn. *Objective 0:* Find the Khajiit caravan's overturned cart west of Old Hroldan Inn |
| 20 |  | I discovered what appears to be the Khajiit caravan's overturned cart along the river west of Old Hroldan Inn. If I fish here, I may be able to recover the lost bottles of aged flin. *Objective 10:* Fish up Ri'saad's lost bottles of aged flin (0/3) |
| 50 |  | I've managed to fish up all of the rare bottles of aged flin that were lost in the river. I should return them to Ri'saad to fulfill the bounty. *Objective 200:* Speak to Ri'saad |
| 200 | ☑ | I gave Ri'saad the lost bottles of aged flin. In return, he paid me with an enchanted ring that aids the wearer in moving quickly and silently. The aged flin must have been very special indeed. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Misc_Khajiit stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Misc_Khajiit`.

# Skyrim:Spread the Love

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Distribute religious [literature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara") to the citizens of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Dinya Balu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinya_Balu "Skyrim:Dinya Balu") |
| Location(s): | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") |
| Reward: | Random Potion |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Dinya Balu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinya_Balu "Skyrim:Dinya Balu")) |
| ID: | FreeformRiften05 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love") | | |

Dinya Balu has one more errand...

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Dinya Balu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinya_Balu "Skyrim:Dinya Balu").
2. Give out 20 *[The Warmth of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara")* missives in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
3. Return to Dinya Balu.

### The Warmth of Mara

Talk to [Dinya Balu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinya_Balu "Skyrim:Dinya Balu") after [The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love") quest and you will be able to provide her with some additional assistance. She will tell you *"[Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") is drowning in a sea of sin and wickedness and it's my personal mission to let everyone know that the warmth of Mara can see them through."* Now, she needs a messenger to bring Mara's words to these poor souls by distributing some missives. Then, she will give you twenty *[The Warmth of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara")* bulletins to give out to the citizens of Riften. You will need to hand out all twenty to complete the quest. Before you start the work, you may ask Dinya for some tips on who might accept the bulletins. She will tell you *"Almost anyone in Riften is in dire need of those missives."* However, it would be wise to keep away from [Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep") and the city guards.

There are a total of thirty-seven people that will accept the missives. You can talk to them *"Here, brother/sister. Blessings of Mara upon you."* Although their reactions vary widely, they will always accept them.

| [The Ragged Flagon - Cistern](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon_-_Cistern "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon - Cistern") | [Vipir the Fleet](/wiki/Skyrim:Vipir_the_Fleet "Skyrim:Vipir the Fleet") | *"Are you out of your mind?"* |
| [The Scorched Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Scorched_Hammer "Skyrim:The Scorched Hammer") | [Asbjorn Fire-Tamer](/wiki/Skyrim:Asbjorn_Fire-Tamer "Skyrim:Asbjorn Fire-Tamer") | *"Oh, well thank you. I'll try and read this if I can."* |
| [The Scorched Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Scorched_Hammer "Skyrim:The Scorched Hammer") | [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund") | *"Thank you for the blessing, I'll put this to good use."* |
| [Valindor's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor%27s_House "Skyrim:Valindor's House") | [Valindor](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor "Skyrim:Valindor") | *"Seems like a noble cause, I'll look it over."* |

Return to Dinya and tell her that you've given away all the missives. She will be quite pleased *"Oh, splendid! Just splendid! Mara smiles upon us this day."* Then, she will reward you with a random potion.

## Notes

- After you've delivered the 20 missives and return to Dinya Balu, you'll be presented with a dialogue option that says you've run out of missives and require more. If you select this option instead of saying you've delivered them all, Dinya will praise your diligence and give you 5 more missives, which can optionally be passed out. When you deliver each of these "extra" missives, the "Completed" quest update notification will reappear, along with the (total/20) count (i.e. 25/20 after you've delivered the last one). However, if you return to Dinya after delivering the extra missives and tell her you've delivered them all, the dialogue and reward will be identical to what you would have received had you not delivered the extra ones. While it doesn't hurt you to do this, there's no actual benefit. Furthermore, you may or may not be given the "extra" option again; some players report seeing this happen while others report that they only got the option once. It appears as though an additional reward may have been intended but was never actually implemented.

## Bugs

- [From-Deepest-Fathoms](/wiki/Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms "Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms") is incorrectly referred to as "brother" when handing her a flier.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- After handing over 19 missives, the option to hand over the 20th may not show. The quest is stuck at this point, and the only way to advance is through console.
  - The 20th missive should still be in your inventory. If you drop it then talk to Dinya, you should be able to ask for extra missives. After this you should be able to deliver the last missive and complete the quest.
- Sometimes, you can give a pamphlet to someone you've already given it to. Quitting and reloading seems to trigger it fairly reliably, but that doesn't appear to be the only factor; certain combinations of saving and reloading can also cause the bug without quitting.
  - Reloading the same save a second time fixes the issue.

## Quest Stages

| Spread the Love (FreeformRiften05) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Distribute the Warmth of Mara within Riften (<Global=FFRiften05Served>/20) |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Return to Dinya |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 25, 200, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften05 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften05`.

# Skyrim:Staada Quest

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Meet with a mysterious figure regarding a [mad wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoron "Skyrim:Thoron")'s failed ritual.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") |
| Location(s): | Near [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")'s Great Arch |
| Reward: | Possibly [Staada's Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Staada%27s_Helmet "Skyrim:Staada's Helmet") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE025\_StaadaQuest |
| Added by: | [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") |

The mysterious figure

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Meet with the mysterious author of the note.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Shortly after completing [Restoring Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoring_Order "Skyrim:Restoring Order"), you will be approached by a courier and given the note *[A Request to Meet](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Request_to_Meet "Skyrim:A Request to Meet")*. Travel to the specified location - the coast under Solitude's Great Arch - and you'll find a Golden Saint named [Staada](/wiki/Skyrim:Staada "Skyrim:Staada"). Speaking with her, you can give her the [Sheogorath-Shaped Amber](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath-Shaped_Amber "Skyrim:Sheogorath-Shaped Amber"), the [Sword of Jyggalag](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword_of_Jyggalag "Skyrim:Sword of Jyggalag"), or neither.

If you choose to give her either the amber or the sword, she will give you her helmet as a reward, then disappear. Keeping both items will turn her hostile, but you can use the amber to learn a permanent summon spell for her (see [notes](#Notes) section). Keeping both items will also forfeit acquiring Staada's Helmet but you will still have both the Sword of Jyggalag and the Sheogorath-Shaped Amber.

## Notes

- If you kept the Sheogorath-Shaped Amber it can be used at the [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge"). Warning, the Sheogorath-Shaped Amber will be destroyed upon choosing one of these options. These combinations do not require the use of a [Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Sigil Stone"). The Staada summoned at the Forge using the Emerald will be hostile.
  - Sheogorath-Shaped Amber + [Emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald") will resummon [Staada](/wiki/Skyrim:Staada "Skyrim:Staada") for another battle.
  - Sheogorath-Shaped Amber + [Ruined Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book") + [Bliss Bug Thorax](/wiki/Skyrim:Bliss_Bug_Thorax "Skyrim:Bliss Bug Thorax") + [Sabre Cat Pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Pelt "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Pelt") will give you a spell tome to summon Staada.
  - Sheogorath-Shaped Amber + Roll Of Paper + Charcoal will give you a scroll to summon Staada only once.

## Bugs

- It is possible to obtain infinite copies of Staada's Helmet. After choosing to give Staada the Sword of Jyggalag, you can exit the conversation and drop the sword before it is removed from your inventory. You will still receive the helmet and can pick up the sword again to repeat the glitch.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.318, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Staada Quest (ccBGSSSE025\_StaadaQuest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 0 |  | *Objective 0:* Read the request to meet |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Locate the author of the mysterious note |
| 11 |  |  |
| 50 |  |  |
| 100 |  |  |
| 200 |  |  |
| 300 | ☑ |  |
| 301 | ☒ |  |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE025_StaadaQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE025_StaadaQuest`.

# Skyrim:Stabilized

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Help [Shadr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadr "Skyrim:Shadr") clear his debt with [Sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(person) "Skyrim:Sapphire (person)").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Shadr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadr "Skyrim:Shadr") |
| Location(s): | Riften |
| Reward: | Leveled gold or a leveled [Potion of Invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Brief_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Brief Invisibility") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Shadr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadr "Skyrim:Shadr")) |
| ID: | FreeformRiften22 |
| Suggested Level: | Any |
| Difficulty: | Easy |

Sapphire demands Shadr pay his debts

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Observe the conversation between [Sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(person) "Skyrim:Sapphire (person)") and [Shadr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadr "Skyrim:Shadr").
2. Speak with Shadr.
3. Speak with Sapphire and either [pay or persuade](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Skill_Usage "Skyrim:Speech") her to clear the debt.
4. Return to Shadr.

### Feeling Blue

Upon your initial entry to [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), a conversation will take place between [Sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(person) "Skyrim:Sapphire (person)"), a member of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), and [Shadr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadr "Skyrim:Shadr"). She is berating him for not paying his debt, to which he replies that he couldn't because his shipment was attacked. Sapphire alludes to the fact that she was behind it, but doesn't forgive his debt and demands that he pay it. She then walks off towards [The Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb").
Shadr is usually on the bridge near the north entry gate (either standing or sitting on the bench), and when you talk to him he will explain his situation. You may then offer to assist him.

### Dealing with Sapphire

When you speak with Sapphire you have a number of options for rectifying the situation:

:   **If you are not a member of the Thieves Guild:** You are presented with the options of [persuading](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Skill_Usage "Skyrim:Speech") Sapphire to clear the debt or paying it yourself.
:   **If you are a member of the Thieves Guild:** You will be presented with the option to be cut in for a leveled amount of gold, or make her forget the debt. Both options are related to threatening to expose her scheme to [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf").
:   **If you are the Guildmaster:** Sapphire will apologize about the scam and claim that she was going to talk with [Delvin](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") about cutting the guild into the deal. You can either tell her to forget about the debt or split the take with her. If you accept the cut-in, you still need to return to Shadr to complete the quest.

### Reward

If you were successful in having Sapphire erase the debt, return to Shadr who is grateful and gives you a leveled [potion of invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Brief_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Brief Invisibility"). This will also increase Shadr's [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") towards you, meaning that you may be able to take items from the [Riften Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Stables "Skyrim:Riften Stables"), including borrowing a [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses"). If you take Sapphire's offer, whether as a Thieves Guild member or the guildmaster, your cut will be a leveled amount of gold.

| Levels | Payoff |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Bugs

- Sapphire has speech options, but none of them perform the proper checks to see if you could succeed. This makes persuading her always succeed by default, no matter what level your [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill is.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=15507))
- In order to successfully intimidate Sapphire into dropping the debt, you need a Speech level which is unattainable by normal means, as the game setting value for intimidation of foolhardy NPCs is out of balance with the other settings.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19173))
- Completing this quest will allow you to ride the horses at [Riften Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Stables "Skyrim:Riften Stables") for free, due to the horses being owned by the stables faction specifically. The problem is that horses cost 1,000 gold, making them way too valuable to let stablemasters let you ride them for free after completing a small favor.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19062)) The ownership of the horses was changed to just Hofgrir, rather than the faction, preventing this issue.
- Sapphire may not talk to you during this quest.
  -  Opening up the console and using the command `resetquest freeformriften22` followed by `setstage freeformriften22 10` re-enables the quest trigger dialogue with Shadr. Don't simply reject helping him (as it triggers the bug) and just talk to Sapphire as usual and the quest will proceed as normal. If you do want to reject helping Shadr (and forfeit the quest reward), you will need to use `stopquest freeformriften22` to get Sapphire to leave the Bee and Barb and move to [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon_-_Cistern "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon - Cistern").
- Telling Shadr you won't help him still pays you the reward and counts toward the Thane quest even though it shouldn't.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, addresses this issue. A script variable to prevent that from happening was missing and out-of-date.
- The quest may not shut down properly if you refuse to help Shadr with his debt.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Stabilized (FreeformRiften22) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Speak to Sapphire about Shadr's debt |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Return to Shadr |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 200, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften22 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften22`.

# Skyrim:Stables

## Overview

Whiterun Stables

 This page lists all the **stables** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"), where [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses") can be bought.

:    **[Katla's Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Katla%27s_Farm "Skyrim:Katla's Farm")** — A small farm and stable along the Karth River, outside of Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Katla%27s+Farm)
:    **[Markarth Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_Stables "Skyrim:Markarth Stables")** — A stable located outside Markarth, opposite the entrance. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Markarth+Stables)
:    **[Riften Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Stables "Skyrim:Riften Stables")** — A stable outside the northern entrance to Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Riften+Stables)
:   **[Solitude Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Stables "Skyrim:Solitude Stables")** — The stable serving the city of Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude+Stables)
:    **[Whiterun Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables")** — A stable just outside the gates of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun+Stables)
:    **[Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables")** — A stable outside of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windhelm+Stables)

# Skyrim:Staff Enchanter

## Overview

The Staff Enchanter

Myrwatch Staff Enchanter

The **Staff Enchanter**, found in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)"), is used to create enchanted staves. It is initially located behind a locked door, requiring you to first complete the [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") quest in order to gain access.

## Related Quests

- **[The Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos"): Complete a mage's quest to reassemble two powerful staves.
- **[Put A Fork In It](/wiki/Skyrim:Put_A_Fork_In_It "Skyrim:Put A Fork In It")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath"): Pass [Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath "Skyrim:Sheogorath")'s trial to earn his staff.

## Other Locations

- A Staff Enchanter can also be found at [Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch_(place) "Skyrim:Myrwatch (place)")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch"), with the added advantage that it can be accessed after only a short [introductory quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch_(quest) "Skyrim:Myrwatch (quest)") without ever having dealt with Neloth.
- A Staff Enchanter can also be found at [Bloodchill Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Cavern "Skyrim:Bloodchill Cavern")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Manor "Skyrim:Bloodchill Manor"). The introductory quest for this enchanter is far more difficult, involving a fight against leveled enemies.

## Craftable Staves

The Staff Enchanter does not require the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") skill, but still increases the skill when used. In order to create an enchanted staff, you must possess an [unenchanted staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves#Craftable_Staves "Skyrim:Staves") of the type desired (unenchanted staves may be purchased from [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth")), know the [spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells "Skyrim:Spells") with which you wish to enchant the staff, and possess enough [heart stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") needed to enchant the staff.

There is no requirement that you be able to cast the spell you wish to use to enchant the staff; merely having read the spell tome for it is enough. Not all spells can be enchanted. The number of heart stones used to enchant the staff has no effect on the amount of Enchanting skill experience earned.

The [Staff of Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath_(item) "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath (item)") can be crafted here as part of the [Staff of Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). The enchanted versions of the [Arm of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Arm_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Arm of the Moon") and the [Arm of the Sun](/wiki/Skyrim:Arm_of_the_Sun "Skyrim:Arm of the Sun") can be crafted here as part of the [Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos") Creation.

### Alteration

These use an [unenchanted Alteration staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves#Unenchanted_Alteration_Staff "Skyrim:Staves") as base object.

### Creation Club

Crafting these staves does not require knowledge of any spell. Despite requiring the use of a Staff Enchanter, these items are not added by the Dragonborn DLC and instead come from various [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") Creations.

| Created Staff | Related Quest | [Heart Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Arm of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Arm_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Arm of the Moon")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos") | [The Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos") | 0 | Requires the [Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). This staff uses the unenchanted version of the Arm of the Moon as a base object, and requires a [Green Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Green Sigil Stone") instead of a Heart Stone. |
| [Arm of the Sun](/wiki/Skyrim:Arm_of_the_Sun "Skyrim:Arm of the Sun")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos") | [The Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos") | 0 | Requires the [Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). This staff uses the unenchanted version of the Arm of the Sun as a base object, and requires an [Orange Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Orange Sigil Stone") instead of a Heart Stone. |
| [Staff of Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath_(item) "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath (item)")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath") | [Put A Fork In It](/wiki/Skyrim:Put_A_Fork_In_It "Skyrim:Put A Fork In It") | 2 | Requires the [Staff of Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). No unenchanted staff is needed for the base; instead, you must obtain the [Branch of the Tree of Shades](/wiki/Skyrim:Branch_of_the_Tree_of_Shades "Skyrim:Branch of the Tree of Shades") and [Ciirta's Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Ciirta%27s_Eye "Skyrim:Ciirta's Eye"). |

## Bugs

- Myrwatch's staff enchanter is not affected by the `DLC2StaffEnchantingMult` perk, which causes it to grant 20 times more experience than normal.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.318, addresses this issue. A separate perk is used to reduce the experience gain.
- Bloodchill Manor's staff enchanter *does* use the `DLC2StaffEnchantingMult` perk, but that perk isn't added to the player until they visit Solstheim for the first time. This means that the staff enchanter will grant 20 times more experience than normal until the player visits Solstheim.
- The door to Neloth's staff enchanter blocks navigation when open, which can lead to some of his quests failing to run because he won't leave the room. The collision on the mesh apparently cuts the navmesh when it shouldn't.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. The door mesh has been modified so both halves will pull up into the ceiling to avoid this.

# Skyrim:Stalhrim Source

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Landmark.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Landmark.png) | Landmark: Stalhrim Source ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Stalhrim+Source)) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2StalhrimSource01, DLC2StalhrimSource02 | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| East of [Broken Tusk Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tusk_Mine "Skyrim:Broken Tusk Mine") Southwest of [Mortrag Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Mortrag_Peak "Skyrim:Mortrag Peak") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Stalhrim Deposits](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") | 10 |

The Stalhrim Source

The **Stalhrim Source** is a small outdoor Nordic ruin east of [Broken Tusk Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tusk_Mine "Skyrim:Broken Tusk Mine") and southwest of [Mortrag Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Mortrag_Peak "Skyrim:Mortrag Peak").

## Related Quests

- **[A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim")**: Find a [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper") missing from [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").

## Stalhrim Source

The Stalhrim Source

The only relatively even approach to the area is from the west through a gap in the mountains reached by passing over the rocks west of [White Ridge Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Barrow "Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow") and proceeding north and east, though you may also approach by descending the mountains from other directions. A stone fence runs along the top of the sunken circular ruin, with a gap in the fence on the west side allowing access to the curved stairs. Descending the stairs reveals ten sarcophagi frozen over with [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim"). Three sarcophagi are to the north, three are to the south, two are to the west partly buried in snow, and two are in the center. The eight outer sarcophagi are upright, while the two in the center are horizontal. After you've mined the stalhrim from each of the sarcophagi, you can loot the uncovered [draugr corpses](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers"). One sarcophagus is half-buried in the snow and only the draugr head is visible, but you can still loot it. If [No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned") is finished, each draugr will have up to 5 gems, usually of flawless quality.

## Notes

- The map marker for this location does not appear until after you have read the [Stalhrim Source Map](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Source_Map "Skyrim:Stalhrim Source Map") obtained during the related quest. If you do not read the map before returning it to Baldor, the map marker will be added upon completing the quest.
- If [Deor Woodcutter](/wiki/Skyrim:Deor_Woodcutter "Skyrim:Deor Woodcutter") or [Fanari Strong-Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:Fanari_Strong-Voice "Skyrim:Fanari Strong-Voice") are killed prior to completing the related quest, you will never be able to learn to forge stalhrim yourself. In addition, you will have to discover the Stalhrim Source's location on your own.
- If you attempt to mine the Stalhrim deposits here with only a regular pickaxe in your inventory, a "You need an Ancient Nordic Pickaxe to use this." message will appear on the top left of the screen.
- If you choose to mine the Stalhrim deposits here manually, you can use the [Elemental Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Fury "Skyrim:Elemental Fury") shout to mine them faster. Don't use an enchanted Ancient Nordic Pickaxe, though, or the shout's speed bonus won't work.

## Bugs

- You may be unable to mine the stalhrim deposits after they respawn. They will appear icy, but will only offer the option to "search draugr". **?**
  - Fast traveling away from the cell and then returning should enable the deposits, allowing you to mine them normally.
  - Save, exit to the title screen, and reload. You should be able to mine the deposits again.
  - Equip your Ancient Nordic Pickaxe and swing at the deposits manually.
  - Fast travel to anywhere on Solstheim, then reload. The deposits should be mineable once again.
-  On [PSVR](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_VR "Skyrim:Skyrim VR"), you may need to strike or mine the deposits more often than is necessary in other versions of the game, a few dozen times per ore.

# Skyrim:Standing Stone

## Overview

The three Guardian Stones

The **Standing Stones** are magical stones found in the wilderness which can give your character special abilities and powers. There are thirteen Standing Stones in total, each associated with one of Tamriel's thirteen [constellations](/wiki/Lore:Astronomy#Constellations "Lore:Astronomy"). Usually, only one stone's effects can be active at a time, although you can change which stone is active at any time by activating a different Standing Stone. However, by wearing the [Aetherial Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherial_Crown "Skyrim:Aetherial Crown")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), you may be affected by two Standing Stones concurrently.

The first three stones most players will encounter are the three [Guardian Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Stones "Skyrim:The Guardian Stones"): the Mage Stone, the Thief Stone, and the Warrior Stone. These three stones are found together in a circle along the road to [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") near [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"). Selecting one of these stones allows you to effectively specialize in one group of [skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills"). All of the other stones are located on their own.

## Achievements

[Achievements](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") related to the Standing Stones are:

-  **Blessed** (10 points/Bronze) — Select a Standing Stone blessing
  - You must discover one standing stone, then activate its blessing. This is most easily accomplished using one of the three Guardian Stones.
-  **Standing Stones** (30 points/Silver) — Find 13 Standing Stones
  - You must discover all thirteen of the standing stones (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

## Notes

- The Standing Stones are comparable to the [Birthsign Stones](/wiki/Oblivion:Doomstones#Birthsign_Stones "Oblivion:Doomstones") from [Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion").
- If you are at or near one of the Standing Stones, and bring up the local map, the map title may refer to it as a "Doomstone". Nothing else in the game seems to use this term for these objects, though.
- [Followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") won't pray at a Standing Stone if you order them to do so.
- Reading *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")* will mark the locations of the following Stones on your map: the Guardian Stones, the Ritual Stone, the Shadow Stone, and the Lover Stone.
- Although the loading screen tip states the Apprentice Stone doubles both magicka regeneration and magicka, only magicka regeneration is doubled.
- [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") is boosted by the Thief Stone. Whether this is intentional or not is unclear:
  - Archery is displayed clearly in the Warrior section of the skill menu, and as each menu section contains a consistent six skills, the Thief Stone's governance of Archery breaks that consistency, perhaps suggesting that this is unintentional.
  - Because Archery has been a stealth skill in previous Elder Scrolls games, its playstyle differs from the Warrior's typical melee tactics and synergizes with [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak"), and the Thief would have no offensive skills if not for Archery, some players believe that Archery was intentionally placed under the Thief Stone.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, moves Archery under the Warrior Stone.

## Bugs

- [The Atronach Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Atronach_Stone "Skyrim:The Atronach Stone") has a 50% chance of causing all [Summoning](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Spells "Skyrim:Conjuration Spells") spells and powers to fail. See [Spell Absorption](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Absorption#Bugs "Skyrim:Spell Absorption") for details.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- Reading *An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim* after the Guardian, Ritual, Lover, and Shadow Stones are marked on the map will cause a "Map updated." message to appear on the top left of the screen again, though no new Stones will be marked. **?**
- It is possible to receive the "Standing Stones" achievement by visiting any of the standing stones a total of 13 times rather than finding all 13 (or visiting the Guardian Stones 5 times). This may result in being stated to have visited more than 13 stones, as repeat visits are not taken into account. You must wait for the location to respawn for repeat visits to increment the counter.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
- There is no loading screen for the Tower Stone.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Statue to Meridia

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Shrine.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Shrine.png) | Daedric Shrine: Statue to Meridia ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Statue+to+Meridia)) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| KilkreathRuinsExterior03 | |
| Region | |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | |
| Location | |
| West of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") East of [Clearpine Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearpine_Pond "Skyrim:Clearpine Pond") | |
| Special Features | |
| [Word Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") | [Elemental Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Fury "Skyrim:Elemental Fury") |

Statue to Meridia holding the beacon

The **Statue to Meridia** is the [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Meridia](/wiki/Lore:Meridia "Lore:Meridia").

## Related Quests

- **[The Break of Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Break_of_Dawn "Skyrim:The Break of Dawn")**: Find [Meridia's Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Meridia%27s_Beacon "Skyrim:Meridia's Beacon") and use its light to cleanse her [temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins") of undead.

## Walkthrough

The climb to the shrine is relatively easy. Steps are cut into the mountain, and Meridia's statue is quite visible. The stone structure supporting the statue is built in the fashion of a stepped pyramid. The door to the [corrupted remains of Meridia's temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins") is built into the base of the shrine to the west, but will only be accessible after the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Break_of_Dawn "Skyrim:The Break of Dawn") is initiated. Visiting this location will start the quest if not previously begun.

A short distance up the mountain northeast of the statue is a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") with a word for the [Elemental Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Fury "Skyrim:Elemental Fury") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Bugs

- The word wall here may not work. **?**
  - Either save, exit to the title screen, and reload, or fast travel away and back again.

# Skyrim:Statue to Meridia

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Shrine.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Shrine.png) | Daedric Shrine: Statue to Meridia ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Statue+to+Meridia)) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| KilkreathRuinsExterior03 | |
| Region | |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | |
| Location | |
| West of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") East of [Clearpine Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearpine_Pond "Skyrim:Clearpine Pond") | |
| Special Features | |
| [Word Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") | [Elemental Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Fury "Skyrim:Elemental Fury") |

Statue to Meridia holding the beacon

The **Statue to Meridia** is the [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Meridia](/wiki/Lore:Meridia "Lore:Meridia").

## Related Quests

- **[The Break of Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Break_of_Dawn "Skyrim:The Break of Dawn")**: Find [Meridia's Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Meridia%27s_Beacon "Skyrim:Meridia's Beacon") and use its light to cleanse her [temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins") of undead.

## Walkthrough

The climb to the shrine is relatively easy. Steps are cut into the mountain, and Meridia's statue is quite visible. The stone structure supporting the statue is built in the fashion of a stepped pyramid. The door to the [corrupted remains of Meridia's temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins") is built into the base of the shrine to the west, but will only be accessible after the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Break_of_Dawn "Skyrim:The Break of Dawn") is initiated. Visiting this location will start the quest if not previously begun.

A short distance up the mountain northeast of the statue is a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") with a word for the [Elemental Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Fury "Skyrim:Elemental Fury") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Bugs

- The word wall here may not work. **?**
  - Either save, exit to the title screen, and reload, or fast travel away and back again.

# Skyrim:Steal, Thugs hunt player

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Experience the consequences of stealing from someone.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | WIAddItem03 |

Contract carried by thugs

## Walkthrough

If you steal an item, the victim of the theft may subsequently send a number (generally three) of [hired thugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Hired_Thug "Skyrim:Hired Thug") to hunt you down. They will casually approach you, but be ready because they will attack you after speaking to you. The thugs will be carrying a [contract](/wiki/Skyrim:Contract_(Theft) "Skyrim:Contract (Theft)") which reveals the name of the victim who hired the thugs.

## Notes

- The item in question can either be stolen from a location or pickpocketed, and you do not have to be seen; an unnoticed theft can still activate the contract. Furthermore, the contract can be from someone who is related to or affiliated with the one you stole from (not the NPC themselves).
- Almost every NPC in the game can send thugs after you.
- Other than stealing, killing someone may also cause a relative to send thugs after you (see [Revenge, Hired Thugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Revenge,_Hired_Thugs "Skyrim:Revenge, Hired Thugs")).

## Bugs

- If you steal an item from someone and kill them straight afterwards, they can still hire thugs to come after you (e.g., a dead [Forsworn Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart") may take out a contract on you for pickpocketing his [heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Briar_Heart "Skyrim:Briar Heart")).
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.
- A theft contract may be mistakenly assigned in place of a [murder contract](/wiki/Skyrim:Contract_(Murder) "Skyrim:Contract (Murder)"). **?**

## Quest Stages

- All of the quest stages are empty: 0, 10, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage WIAddItem03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest WIAddItem03`.

# Skyrim:Stealer of Souls

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. | |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The Kagrumez Gauntlet](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Kagrumez_Gauntlet "Skyrim:The Kagrumez Gauntlet") | | |

The Soul Stealer Arrows

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the [letter from Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Calcelmo "Skyrim:Letter from Calcelmo").
2. Retrieve the [Soul Stealer Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Stealer_Arrow "Skyrim:Soul Stealer Arrow") from [Kagrumez](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrumez "Skyrim:Kagrumez").

## Detailed Walkthrough

**Note: This quest, along with a [Letter from Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Calcelmo "Skyrim:Letter from Calcelmo") and the [Dwemer Arrow Diagram](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Arrow_Diagram "Skyrim:Dwemer Arrow Diagram"), were originally added to your inventory upon installing the [Skyrim:Arcane Archer Pack](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Archer_Pack "Skyrim:Arcane Archer Pack") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). With the release of the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition"), the letter and quest no longer appear. You can still acquire [Soul Stealer Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Stealer_Arrow "Skyrim:Soul Stealer Arrow") and the Dwemer Arrow Diagram from [Kagrumez](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrumez "Skyrim:Kagrumez") on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").**

Kagrumez is a high-level dungeon with a minimum enemy level of 25. As such, it is recommended that you prepare for a tough fight if you plan to complete this quest at a lower level. The majority of the dungeon is initially inaccessible, so you will first need to complete [The Kagrumez Gauntlet](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Kagrumez_Gauntlet "Skyrim:The Kagrumez Gauntlet"), a fetch quest which requires you to gather [Kagrumez Resonance Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrumez_Resonance_Gem "Skyrim:Kagrumez Resonance Gem") from all over Solstheim. You need to collect four gems in order to unlock the final chamber in Kagrumez.

Once you have unlocked the final chamber, you can find several Soul Stealer Arrows next to the [Dwarven Black Bow of Fate](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Black_Bow_of_Fate "Skyrim:Dwarven Black Bow of Fate"). Pick up the arrows to complete the quest. You will now be able to craft Soul Stealer Arrows at any [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge").

## Quest Stages

| Stealer of Souls (ccBGSSSE002\_SoulStealerQuest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |

| 10 |  | I've received a letter and a diagram of an ancient Dwemer artifact, an arrow that appears to be crafted from Soul Gems. I should retrieve this artifact and learn how to create them. *Objective :* Travel to Solstheim |
| 20 |  | I've received a letter and a diagram of an ancient Dwemer artifact, an arrow that appears to be crafted from Soul Gems. I should retrieve this artifact and learn how to create them. *Objective :* Find the Soul Stealer Arrows |
| 30 | ☑ | I've found the ancient Dwemer Soul Stealer arrows in Kagrumez, and am now able to craft them. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 25.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE002_SoulStealerQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE002_SoulStealerQuest`.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Aela](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress").
2. Retrieve the [Silver Hand Stratagem](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand_Stratagem "Skyrim:Silver Hand Stratagem").
3. Return to Aela.

## Detailed Walkthrough

To proceed in taking revenge for [Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor"), [Aela](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela "Skyrim:Aela") suggests that you steal Silver Hand plans to intercept any actions they might take. You will be sent to a radiant location, where a regiment of Silver Hand will be guarding a leader and his plans. Whether you sneak through the camp or kill everyone in your path is completely optional.

### Reward

| Levels[†](#intnote_LevelNote) | Reward[‡](#intnote_RewardBug) | USLEEP Reward |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 100 | 100 |
| 10–19 | 150 | 150 |
| 20–29 | 300 | 200 |
| 30–39 | 300 | 250 |
| 40+ | 300 | 300 |

[†](#note_LevelNote)Level is based on when the player completed the previous quest (or level one for the first quest), not the player's level when receiving the quest or its reward.

[‡](#note_RewardBug)The reward amounts for radiant Companions quests do not progress as intended.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=20007))

## Bugs

- The Silver Hand Stratagem may be placed in an inaccessible location, or in an inaccessible chest instead of the proper boss container at the assigned radiant dungeon.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
  - It has been reported that the [console command](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") `movetoqt CR10` can resolve this issue, specifically if the target location is Treva's Watch (see talk page). The use of console commands may have unintended effects.
- The Stratagem may appear in a random dungeon, even if you've never been given the quest.
- The Stratagem may appear on the floor in Jorrvaskr at the location you initially gave it to Aela. Picking The Stratagem up will result in it being bound to your inventory (as it is a quest item).
- After returning and reporting to Aela, your quest will be acknowledged as complete in the journal, but it may remain in your active quest list. If this happens, Aela will not give you any further Silver Hand radiant quest to do (but will still give [Skyrim:Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination "Skyrim:Animal Extermination") quests). This bug can occurr with any Silver Hand radiant quest. **?**

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CR10 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CR10`.

# Skyrim:Steamcrag Camp

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Giant Camp.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Giant_Camp.png) | Giant Camp: Steamcrag Camp ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Steamcrag+Camp)) | | |

Steamcrag Camp

**Steamcrag Camp** is a [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") south of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

Steamcrag Camp

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Giant "Skyrim:Bounty: Giant")**: Kill a problematic [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") for a bounty reward. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Walkthrough

One [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") and up to two [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") occupy the camp. An [official warning](/wiki/Skyrim:Official_warning "Skyrim:Official warning") posted on the nearby signpost grants the giant permission to camp there and warns citizens not to interfere with him. In the center of the camp is a large campfire with two [horse haunches](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Haunch "Skyrim:Horse Haunch") and a [charred skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Meat "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Meat") cooking beside it. A [giant club](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Club "Skyrim:Giant Club") is near the campfire (see [bugs](#Bugs)). Southwest of the fire is a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide") and an [ice wolf pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Ice Wolf Pelt"), while to the north is a [dead Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_(dead) "Skyrim:Khajiit (dead)"). To the northwest near a large rock is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and two [mammoth cheese bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl"); taking the cheese bowls counts as theft. Two haunches of raw [horse meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Meat "Skyrim:Horse Meat") and an unowned mammoth cheese bowl sit on a rock to the right. On the rocks above is a fire with a dead [wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") and a dead [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses") cooking on top. The [wolf's pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Wolf Pelt") can be looted from its body, while the [horse's hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Hide "Skyrim:Horse Hide") lies beside the fire. [Jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes") and [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") grow in the vicinity.

To the southeast, near the road and the signpost, is a destroyed carriage with another dead Khajiit, a dead horse, various common books strewn about, an adept-locked chest, a barrel containing ingredients, several food sacks, and a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"). The dead Khajiit near the campfire may have come from this caravan to attempt to barter with the giant.

## Notes

- Due to the camp's proximity to the dragon lair at [Bonestrewn Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonestrewn_Crest "Skyrim:Bonestrewn Crest"), you may attract the attention of the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") while dealing with the giant and mammoths. This may be either helpful or harmful depending on whether the parties attack you or each other.
- South-southeast of the camp, atop a large rocky hill, is a [shrine of Akatosh](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Akatosh "Skyrim:Shrines") on a stone bier. The three leveled [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") near the surrounding pillars will rise and attack when you approach the bier. A leveled war axe and a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Breathing Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Breathing_Water "Skyrim:Breathing Water")* are next to the shrine.

## Bugs

- The mammoth cheese containers here are erroneously marked as owned by the giants.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.
- The giant club cannot be used by you, but can be picked up by a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") if you order them to do so. However, it will then be impossible to remove it from their inventory.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.


---
