# Skyrim:Steamscorch Mine

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Mine: Steamscorch Mine ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Steamscorch+Mine)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Catalogue of Armor Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Armor_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Armor Enchantments")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| KynesgroveSteamscorchGullyMine | |
| Region | |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | |
| Location | |
| [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Tanning Racks](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning") | 1 |
| # of [Smelters](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") | 1 |
| # of [Wood Chopping Blocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood") | 1 |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Malachite](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite_Ore "Skyrim:Malachite Ore") | 7 |

Steamscorch Mine

**Steamscorch Mine** is a small [malachite](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") in northeastern [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove"). It contains only one zone, *[Steamscorch Mine](#Steamscorch_Mine)*.

[Kjeld](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjeld "Skyrim:Kjeld") will [buy malachite ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore") from you.

## Residents

| Steamscorch Mine Camp |
| --- |
| [Ganna Uriel](/wiki/Skyrim:Ganna_Uriel "Skyrim:Ganna Uriel")  [Gemma Uriel](/wiki/Skyrim:Gemma_Uriel "Skyrim:Gemma Uriel")  [Klija Wolf-Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Klija_Wolf-Claw "Skyrim:Klija Wolf-Claw") [CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions") †  [Roggi Knot-Beard](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggi_Knot-Beard "Skyrim:Roggi Knot-Beard") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") \*  [Stormcloak Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Guard "Skyrim:Stormcloak Guard") |

\* Only becomes available as a follower after you complete a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)") to locate his lost [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggi%27s_Ancestral_Shield "Skyrim:Roggi's Ancestral Shield").
† Only appears if the [Civil War Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") is installed on a character who has not yet chosen a side in the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). See [bugs](#Bugs).

## Related Quests

- **[Battle of the Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_the_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of the Champions")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions"): A battle between two [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") champions is about to begin.
- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

North of the [Braidwood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Braidwood_Inn "Skyrim:Braidwood Inn") is a small path passing a camp that leads east and north up a hill to the entrance of the mine. Outside the mine is a [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter"), three owned [malachite ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite_Ingot "Skyrim:Malachite Ingot") on the end of a cart, and one owned piece of [malachite ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite_Ore "Skyrim:Malachite Ore") on a crate, with a second unowned piece of malachite ore behind another crate farther to the west. There are no hostiles in or around the mine, although after the quest [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") often fly overhead. The mine path continues onward to a dragon burial mound east of Kynesgrove (related to the quest [A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark")).

Steamscorch mine camp

North of the inn and west of the entrance to the mine is the miners' camp. It consists of a central campfire around which are three small tents, each containing an unowned bedroll. North of the fire are two food barrels with a rack holding nine owned [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"). Northeast of the fire is a vegetable patch where ten [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), four [gourds](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), six [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), and eight [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") grow. A [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") and a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") are on the fringe of the camp, and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") is by the northwestern corner of the inn. A [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") plant and a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush can be found around the camp.

### Steamscorch Mine

Mine interior

Inside the mine are seven malachite ore veins ( on the map) and twenty-one patches of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"). The first two malachite ore veins are just inside the mine on either side of the main path, with an empty chest on the right of the tunnel; the other five veins are deeper in. The tunnel opens up to a small area with a table (**A** on the map) holding a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Catalogue of Armor Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Armor_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Armor Enchantments")*, a bottle of wine, and a random [healing potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). A pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") can be found on the ground by the table. The mine then splits into two parallel tunnels, both of which lead to the area at the end. The left tunnel contains another table with several food barrels and sacks as well as a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots"), while the right tunnel leads to a side tunnel containing a malachite ore vein. The remaining four malachite ore veins are all in the area at the end of the tunnels; two of the veins are on the ground, and two more are accessible by climbing the scaffolding in the area.

The mine is worked by a few NPCs and is often patrolled by the [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") mage [Dravynea the Stoneweaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea_the_Stoneweaver "Skyrim:Dravynea the Stoneweaver"). She resides at the nearby inn and offers a [miscellaneous quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea%27s_Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Dravynea's Frost Salts") to bring her [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") in return for training in the school of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"). Dravynea also states it is her job to keep the mine safe and prevent it from collapsing.

## Notes

- Once you have completed the quest to locate [Roggi's Ancestral Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggi%27s_Ancestral_Shield "Skyrim:Roggi's Ancestral Shield"), the next time you visit the mine, the shield will be at the top of the ramp against the rear wall of the mine; it will not be marked as owned and will therefore be free to take.

## Bugs

- If Klija appears at Kynesgrove but you then side with the Imperial Legion and kill her during the quest [Battle of the Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_the_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of the Champions"), this version of her will not be disabled and she will continue to live at the camp. **?**
- One of the pieces of malachite ore outside the mine may be buried under the ground, making it irretrievable.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
- There is a broken navmesh in this mine, making the back 1/3 of the mine largely inaccessible to the NPCs when they work here.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.

## Maps

A

Steamscorch Mine

# Skyrim:Steepfall Burrow

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Steepfall Burrow ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Steepfall+Burrow)) | | |

| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 2 |

| Console Location Code(s) | |

| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") | 1 |

Lower Steepfall Burrow

**Steepfall Burrow** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") and [ice wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf "Skyrim:Ice Wolf"). It contains only one zone, *[Steepfall Burrow](#Steepfall_Burrow)*.

Although the interior of the cave is named "Steepfall Burrow", the map markers for the two entrances are named "Steepfall Burrow" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Steepfall+Burrow&zoom=14&legacy=true) and "Lower Steepfall Burrow" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lower+Steepfall+Burrow&zoom=14&legacy=true), counting as two separate locations for the "Locations Discovered" statistic. To fully explore the cave, you must enter via the upper "Steepfall Burrow" entrance.

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The upper cave entrance is along a winding dirt path in the mountainous region west of [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad"), near the northern coast of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar").

### Steepfall Burrow

Upon entering, there is a ledge on your right with a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush; a second bush is ahead. The tunnel heads south before turning east and opening into a cavern with a natural bridge across a deep drop into water. A frost troll is on the other side of the bridge. Beyond is a tunnel rising to the east to a small chamber with another frost troll. North of the chamber is a small passage where a skeleton is laid out with a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Mystery of Talara, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_v3 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, v3")* and a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), and [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"). In the corner opposite is an unlocked boss [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") with a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a random [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") in front and a snowberry bush at either end. The drop from the bridge into the water is survivable, and leads to the lower section of the cave.

At the bottom of the pool is an apprentice-locked chest with a random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") next to it on the southwest side, while a small coin purse and a random [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer") and [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") are near some mammoth ribs on the north side. Directly under the bridge, on the west side of the pool, is a short underwater tunnel leading to a chamber where a small pack of ice wolves lairs; one of the wolves is next to where you emerge from the tunnel. South of where you surface is an unlocked chest to the left of an earthen ramp leading up to the ledge above. On the ledge is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") and a snowberry bush to the right, while to the left is a dead [hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") lying near a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") and a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"). Just north of where you surface is a small tunnel leading to the "Lower Steepfall Burrow" exit at the bottom of the mountain near the shore.

## Notes

- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations.

Lower Steepfall Burrow

**Steepfall Burrow** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") and [ice wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf "Skyrim:Ice Wolf"). It contains only one zone, *[Steepfall Burrow](#Steepfall_Burrow)*.

Although the interior of the cave is named "Steepfall Burrow", the map markers for the two entrances are named "Steepfall Burrow" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Steepfall+Burrow&zoom=14&legacy=true) and "Lower Steepfall Burrow" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lower+Steepfall+Burrow&zoom=14&legacy=true), counting as two separate locations for the "Locations Discovered" statistic. To fully explore the cave, you must enter via the upper "Steepfall Burrow" entrance.

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The upper cave entrance is along a winding dirt path in the mountainous region west of [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad"), near the northern coast of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar").

### Steepfall Burrow

Upon entering, there is a ledge on your right with a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush; a second bush is ahead. The tunnel heads south before turning east and opening into a cavern with a natural bridge across a deep drop into water. A frost troll is on the other side of the bridge. The drop from the bridge into the water is survivable, and leads to the lower section of the cave.

At the bottom of the pool is an apprentice-locked chest with a random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") next to it on the southwest side, while a small coin purse and a random [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer") and [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") are near some mammoth ribs on the north side. Directly under the bridge, on the west side of the pool, is a short underwater tunnel leading to a chamber where a small pack of ice wolves lairs; one of the wolves is next to where you emerge from the tunnel. South of where you surface is an unlocked chest to the left of an earthen ramp leading up to the ledge above. On the ledge is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") and a snowberry bush to the right, while to the left is a dead [hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") lying near a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") and a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"). Just north of where you surface is a small tunnel leading to the "Lower Steepfall Burrow" exit at the bottom of the mountain near the shore.

# Skyrim:Stendarr's Beacon

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Imperial Tower.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Imperial_Tower.png) | Imperial Tower: Stendarr's Beacon ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Stendarr%27s+Beacon)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes (See [bugs](#Bugs)) |

| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |

Stendarr's Beacon

**Stendarr's Beacon** is a small [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") southeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

## Walkthrough

The path to the beacon branches south from the main road southeast of Riften, opposite the path toward [Black-Briar Lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Lodge "Skyrim:Black-Briar Lodge"). The path passes another path leading northwest to [Broken Helm Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Helm_Hollow "Skyrim:Broken Helm Hollow"), and continues south then east before climbing north. At the top, the beacon is ahead to the left. Outside the tower, the three resident [Vigilants of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilant of Stendarr") have set up a makeshift kitchen, complete with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") and a nearby table holding a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"), a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), and a joint of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), with a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") beside the table. A [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") is a few feet west of the cooking spit. Around the back of the tower is a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), with a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") and [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") lying next to it.

Inside the tower, the Vigilants have set up a [shrine of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Shrine of Stendarr") with their bedrolls to the left, one of which has a copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Exodus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Exodus "Skyrim:The Exodus")* resting on it that you may freely take. If you take the stairs to the top of the tower, you will find a large campfire and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot owned by the Vigilants; being seen to loot the chest will turn the Vigilants hostile.

## Notes

- To the southeast, a flag can be seen flying up on the ridge. The path up to the ridge is splashed with blood, and a [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") roams the area. At the base of the flagpole is an apprentice-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") and one or two other pieces of loot, with some humanoid remains nearby. The strongbox doesn't respawn. Under a nearby wolf corpse is a skill book [A Dance in Fire, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v2 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v2").
- At the foot of the next ridge to the east, before turning right onto the blood-stained path upward, there is a second silver ore vein on the right.
- A [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") is west of the tower, and two [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") are east of the tower.
- If you have [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") installed, the cave entrance to [Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon") will be northeast of here.

## Bugs

- To mark this location as cleared, you must kill all three Vigilants in one go. If you leave one or more alive and leave the area for long enough for them to despawn, it will be impossible to clear the tower later, as the three Vigilants never respawn.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, addresses this issue. The incorrectly applied clearable flag has been removed altogether.
- The fix from Unofficial Skyrim Patch 2.0.1 overlooked a major detail. Based on further examination, it appears that the flag's presence was intended as a clearable target for vampire players - several of the Vigilants here are flagged as Bosses, meaning the clearable flag should never have been removed in the first place.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.1, addresses this issue. The previously removed clearable flag has been restored.

# Skyrim:Stillborn Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Stillborn Cave ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Stillborn+Cave)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 18 |
| Occupants | |
| [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [Chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") | |
| Important Treasure | |

| Console Location Code(s) | |
| StillbornCave01 | |

| South-southeast of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") North of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") | 1 |

Stillborn Cave

**Stillborn Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south-southeast of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). It contains only one zone, *[Stillborn Cave](#Stillborn_Cave)*.

## Related Quests

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The cave has two entrances: one along the road to Winterhold and the other farther uphill. An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") can be found northeast of the main entrance.

### Stillborn Cave

The entrance along the road leads into an ice tunnel heading south. The path soon turns to the west, where an ice melt runoff flowing from east to west is carving a rapid stream through the cave. Ahead is a leveled [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") near some [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer")-style fencing in front of an exit to the west. The path follows the north wall around and down to where the chaurus is wandering. It is possible to reach the other side of the stream; however, there is nothing of interest over there. The western exit is an ice tunnel that turns to the south then back to the west before opening into a cave with an alcove to the north containing an unlocked Falmer [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). An exit is found to the west across from where you entered, and around the corner to the south is an empty gated Falmer tent, with a [Falmer hive](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Hive "Skyrim:Falmer Hive") on the wall between the tent and exit. There is a patrolling Falmer behind the tent, and another hiding in the hive. An unlocked Falmer chest is to the right of the tent.

Taking the tunnel to the west, the tunnel turns to the north before opening into a cave with a magic-using Falmer that favors frost magic and another leveled chaurus. At the rear of the cave is a Falmer tent containing an unlocked chest, a [Falmer shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Shield "Skyrim:Falmer Shield"), and a human [skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull "Skyrim:Skull"). From the first cave, the path leads along the south wall around the front of the gated tent, rising behind the tent. Be careful, as there is a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") across the path that activates a [claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Claw "Skyrim:Claw") trap hinged on a pillar to the right. On the right side of the pillar is an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") beside a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Warrior's Charge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrior%27s_Charge "Skyrim:The Warrior's Charge")*. Beyond this, a narrow tunnel heads to the southwest.

The tunnel turns to the northwest, then opens into another cave with a Falmer patrolling. In this cave, there is a caved-in tunnel to the south with a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on the ground in front of it, an exit to the north, and another exit past the Falmer to the west. After a short distance, the tunnel to the north opens into what appears to be an empty cave, with a novice-locked chest in front. However, there are hives in alcoves to your left and right, out of sight, both of which potentially hide Falmer ready to attack; human remains sprawled in front of the chest and riddled with Falmer arrows hint at this ambush.

From the previous cave, taking the exit to the west leads to another ice melt stream flowing north to south. There are several [chaurus egg sacs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs") around this stream. Following the stream south, the passage opens into a large cave with two leveled chaurus and a leveled Falmer boss. There are more egg sacs on both sides of the stream. The path rises along the east wall to an unlocked Falmer chest, hidden behind some fencing above the stream. The exit from this cave is found by following the stream south. This continues until the ceiling again becomes too low to proceed; at this point, there is a path to the east. This passage turns south once more, then leads to the second exit uphill from the first.

## Notes

- An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is a few paces northeast of the first entrance.
- The second entrance isn't marked on your map.
- When reaching the second stream, your internal map will show a tunnel heading north; however, you can't fit through the gap, as the ceiling is too low.
- This is the smallest and brightest cave system containing Falmer, and one of the most convenient and nearest to Winterhold for collecting the Falmer blood required for the quest [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane").
- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations.

## Bugs

- It is possible to get stuck between the pillar on the right of the stream and the west wall of the cave. **?**
  - Reloading a previous save appears to be the only solution, unless you are playing on PC and can use the `tcl` console command.

## Overview

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Supply specific fish to random innkeepers

## Detailed Walkthrough

This is a repetitive quest. [Swims-In-Deep-Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water "Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water") will ask you to supply certain types of fish to randomly chosen innkeepers ([Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") being a possible destination). The quest can be completed four times.

## Quest Stages

| Stocking Up (ccBGSSSE001\_Radiant\_1) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 0 |  | Swims-In-Deep-Water has given me a fishing bounty. I should read what the bounty letter has to say. *Objective 1000:* Read Bounty: Supply of Brook Bass  *Objective 1001:* Read Bounty: Supply of Salmon  *Objective 1002:* Read Bounty: Supply of Catfish  *Objective 1003:* Read Bounty: Supply of Arctic Grayling  *Objective 200:* Speak to <Alias=Innkeeper> |
| 10 |  | <Alias=Innkeeper> is running low on fresh fish for <Alias.PronounPosObj=Innkeeper> patrons and has put out a bounty to replenish <Alias.PronounPosObj=Innkeeper> stock of brook bass. *Objective 0:* Obtain <Global=ccBGSSSE001\_RadiantObjTotal> brook bass for <Alias.ShortName=Innkeeper> in <Alias=Town> |
| 11 |  | <Alias=Innkeeper> is running low on fresh fish for <Alias.PronounPosObj=Innkeeper> patrons and has put out a bounty to replenish <Alias.PronounPosObj=Innkeeper> stock of salmon. *Objective 1:* Obtain <Global=ccBGSSSE001\_RadiantObjTotal> salmon for <Alias.ShortName=Innkeeper> in <Alias=Town> |
| 12 |  | <Alias=Innkeeper> is running low on fresh fish for <Alias.PronounPosObj=Innkeeper> patrons and has put out a bounty to replenish <Alias.PronounPosObj=Innkeeper> stock of catfish. *Objective 2:* Obtain <Global=ccBGSSSE001\_RadiantObjTotal> catfish for <Alias.ShortName=Innkeeper> in <Alias=Town> |

| 200 | ☑ | I supplied <Alias=Innkeeper> with the fish <Alias.Pronoun=Innkeeper> needed. |
| 250 | ☒ | <Alias=Innkeeper> has died, leaving me unable to fulfill the bounty. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Radiant_1 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Radiant_1`.

# Skyrim:Stoking the Flames

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Find 10 [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts") to restore [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund")'s forge.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund") |
| Location(s): | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") |
| Reward: | Leveled Gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund")) |
| ID: | FreeformRiften10 |

Balimund needs Fire Salts for his forge.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund").
2. Gather [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts").
3. Return to Balimund.

## Detailed Walkthrough

If you speak to [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund") at his forge in the center of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") and ask him about how proud he is of his work, he will tell you that the forge is not as good as it used to be. It is supposed to run on [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), but they seem to be wearing off. He estimates that he needs ten fire salts to get the forge back to its original strength:

:   **You seem quite proud of your work.**
:   *"Smithing's been in my blood for generations. I owe my success to my forefathers and their recipe for flame. The secret is my forge. It consumes fire salts, a strange mineral that burns as hot as Red Mountain lava."*
:   **Impressive.**
:   *"Well, it was. Sadly, this forge is dying and I've used the last of my fire salts. If I can't feed it soon, it may grow cold."*
:   **I'll get some for you.**
:   *"You will? Thank you! Ten pinches of fire salts should give me all I need to bring this forge back to life."*
:   **Where can I find fire salts?**
:   *"A flame atronach's body might provide fire salt. They're dangerous creatures that can be summoned by wizards. Of course, it would be much easier to check with an alchemist. They occasionally have them for sale."*

Details on where to find fire salts are provided on the [ingredient page](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts").

Once you have ten salts, return to Balimund and receive a leveled amount of gold:

:   **I've found the fire salts for your forge.**
:   *"Amazing! These must have been very hard to come by. You've saved my business and warmed an old smith's heart. For that, I thank you."*

## Notes

- Even though Balimund says that "only genuine" fire salts will work, they are not like the bloodgrass for the [Vampirism Cure Quest in Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Vampire_Cure "Oblivion:Vampire Cure") (e.g. where bloodgrass purchased in a shop doesn't count). Instead, fire salts from any combination of sources will work—from [flame atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Flame Atronach"), purchased from [merchants](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Skyrim:Merchants"), stolen, and/or crafted at the [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge").
- Even though the in-game story is that the fire salts make the forge stronger, neither Balimund's merchant inventory nor the things you can craft at his forge receive any upgrade in quality after completing this quest. The amount of money in his store does increase, as if you had invested in his store (if you have already invested in it, or if you invest later, the two effects do not stack).

## Quest Stages

| Stoking the Flames (FreeformRiften10) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Bring 10 fire salts to Balimund (<Global=FFR10SaltCount>/10) *(re-displayed as each fire salt is acquired or removed)* |
|  |  | *(Once all ten fire salts are acquired)* *Objective 20:* Return to Balimund |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften10 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften10`.

# Skyrim:Stonehill Bluff

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Giant Camp.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Giant_Camp.png) | Giant Camp: Stonehill Bluff ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Stonehill+Bluff)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 2 |
| Occupants | |
| [Giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| StonehillBluffExterior01, StonehillBluffExterior02, StonehillBluffExterior03 | |
| Region | |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | |
| Location | |
| South-southwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") North-northeast of [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud") | |

Stonehill Bluff

**Stonehill Bluff** is a [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") south-southwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Giant "Skyrim:Bounty: Giant")**: Kill a problematic [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") for a bounty reward. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial")**: Acquire the materials necessary to repair the [White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)").

## Walkthrough

The camp is at the end of a ravine, with the easiest approach from the east. If *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* is installed and [Heljarchen Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Heljarchen_Hall "Skyrim:Heljarchen Hall") has been built, a short distance uphill west of the hall is a path leading west into the ravine. A [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") guards the ravine. The path features the painted stones, [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes"), and mammoth ribs and skulls typical of giant camps. As you follow the ravine into the camp, you will find a patch of [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") near a patch of [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), with two more white caps in the camp itself.

Two giants (including the guard in the ravine) occupy the camp, which is in a basin surrounded by large rock formations. There are two large campfires with a total of six [charred skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") cooking on fire-hardened stakes. Seven [mammoth cheese bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl") and two unlocked [chests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") are found in the camp, with one chest at the northern end of the basin and the other against the rocks to the east.

## Bugs

- The fungi patches, charred skeevers, and mammoth cheese bowls do not respawn with the rest of the camp. **?**

# Skyrim:Stonehills

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Mine.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Mine.png) | Settlement: Stonehills ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Stonehills)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Stonehills "Lore:Stonehills")) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| StonehillsExterior01, StonehillsExterior02, StonehillsExterior03 | |

| East of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") West of [Dimhollow Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Dimhollow_Crypt "Skyrim:Dimhollow Crypt") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Smelters](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") | 1 |
| # of [Grindstones](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") | 1 |
| # of [Wood Chopping Blocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood") | 1 |
| # of [Stone Quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | 2 |

Stonehills

**Stonehills** is a small mining [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") east of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal").

Stonehills is the encampment for the miners working in [Rockwallow Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Rockwallow_Mine "Skyrim:Rockwallow Mine"), owned by [Thane Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling") of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), with [Sorli's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli%27s_House "Skyrim:Sorli's House") next to the mine. [Sorli the Builder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli_the_Builder "Skyrim:Sorli the Builder") and her spouse, [Pactur](/wiki/Skyrim:Pactur "Skyrim:Pactur"), run the mine and live in the house with their son [Sirgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sirgar "Skyrim:Sirgar"). The camp consists of a group of five small tents arranged around a central campfire, each with a bedroll inside. North of the campfire is a rack with nine [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") hanging from it, with a chicken coop containing two [chicken's nests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") further to the north near a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") and [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter"). Beside the smelter is a cart holding four [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), with six more ingots stacked beside the [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") on the ground. Opposite the cart are a stack of crates with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on top.

Southwest of the campfire is a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), while around the camp are a few patches of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry") bush, and several [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") patches. A waist-high stone wall in poor condition separates the camp from the road, also marking the path to the mine and encampment. The road links [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") to Morthal. The settlement is protected by one [Hjaalmarch guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Guard "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Guard"), who stands outside the mine.

## Stonehills Residents

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | [Sorli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli%27s_House "Skyrim:Sorli's House") | | --- | | **[Pactur](/wiki/Skyrim:Pactur "Skyrim:Pactur")**  **[Sirgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sirgar "Skyrim:Sirgar")**  **[Sorli the Builder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli_the_Builder "Skyrim:Sorli the Builder")** | | | [Rockwallow Mine Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rockwallow_Mine "Skyrim:Rockwallow Mine") | | --- | | **[Gestur Rockbreaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Gestur_Rockbreaker "Skyrim:Gestur Rockbreaker")**  **[Hjaalmarch Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Guard "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Guard")**  **[Jesper](/wiki/Skyrim:Jesper "Skyrim:Jesper")**  **[Swanhvir](/wiki/Skyrim:Swanhvir "Skyrim:Swanhvir")**  **[Teeba-Ei](/wiki/Skyrim:Teeba-Ei "Skyrim:Teeba-Ei")** | |

## Related Quests

- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Payment Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Payment_Delivery "Skyrim:Payment Delivery")**: Tell [Thane Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling") that the late shipment from [Rockwallow Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Rockwallow_Mine "Skyrim:Rockwallow Mine") will be arriving soon.

## Notes

- Unused keys, merchant chests, and NPCs indicate Stonehills was originally intended to be significantly larger than it appears in the final game.
  - Mine workers Jesper, Swanhvir, and Teeba-Ei each carry a key to a longhouse which doesn't exist, suggesting they'd all bunk together in one residence.
  - Another unused key and a locklist indicate mine overseer Gestur Rockbreaker was also meant to live in his own house.
  - Two unused NPCs were also meant to be present here: [Talib](/wiki/Skyrim:Talib "Skyrim:Talib"), the son of Gestur, and [Argi Farseer](/wiki/Skyrim:Argi_Farseer "Skyrim:Argi Farseer"), the sister of [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Idgrod Ravencrone](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_Ravencrone "Skyrim:Idgrod Ravencrone"), the latter of whom would have also had her own house.
  - Finally, another unused key and a merchant chest indicate a blacksmith vendor named **Aleuc**, who no longer exists in NPC form, was also meant to reside at Stonehills.
- As can be seen by their Form IDs, the workers at Stonehills were created before the members of Sorli's family. Moreover, the workers never interact with any member of Sorli's family, who in turn have no unique scenes and only mention each other in passing. Finally, Pactur and Gestur Rockbreaker both act as if they're the mine overseer, while completely ignoring the other's existence.
- During the day, an unusually large number of [blue butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly") and [monarch butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Monarch_Butterfly "Skyrim:Monarch Butterfly") are along the road and path leading to the settlement.
- With the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on, this entire settlement is an excellent place to stock up on iron for [housebuilding](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") purposes.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the 10 iron ingots in the camp as owned.
- Stonehills also [appears](/wiki/Arena:Stonehills "Arena:Stonehills") in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")*.

## Bugs

- If the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") take over [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") as part of the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), Pactur's wife Sorli will be appointed the new jarl and will move to [Highmoon Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Highmoon_Hall "Skyrim:Highmoon Hall") in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). Although Pactur is meant to serve as her steward, she will only bring mine worker Teeba-Ei to Morthal, leaving Pactur in Stonehills. Despite remaining in Stonehills, Pactur's dialogue will change to suggest he is living in Morthal and serving as Sorli's steward.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  - This bug is also fixed by the [Hearthfire add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"). It gives Pactur AI packages that ensure he relocates to Morthal at the appropriate time.
- If the Stormcloaks capture Hjaalmarch as part of the civil war, the new Stormcloak guard stationed here isn't a member of the Stormcloak faction.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

Stony Creek Cave

**Stony Creek Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains only one zone, *[Stony Creek Cave](#Stony_Creek_Cave)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Finn's Lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute "Skyrim:Finn's Lute")**: Return an invaluable [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute_(item) "Skyrim:Finn's Lute (item)") to [Inge Six Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:Inge_Six_Fingers "Skyrim:Inge Six Fingers").
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[The Edge of Ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Edge_of_Ruin "Skyrim:The Edge of Ruin")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruin%27s_Edge "Skyrim:Ruin's Edge"): Find a madwoman's [legendary bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruin%27s_Edge_(item) "Skyrim:Ruin's Edge (item)").
- **[Careless Curation](/wiki/Skyrim:Careless_Curation "Skyrim:Careless Curation")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Find the missing Curate to retrieve the [Mask of Sotha Sil](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Sotha_Sil "Skyrim:Mask of Sotha Sil").

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo").
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave.
- **[Find Shahvee's Amulet of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout.
- **[Harsh Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Harsh_Master "Skyrim:Harsh Master")**: Take care of a runaway crew member.
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The entrance to the cave is near a small pond with a jetty and rowboat to the west. With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found here. Fish from [Temperate Lakes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") can be caught here. The middle of the pond bed features several harvestable [clams](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam_Meat "Skyrim:Clam Meat"). The cave entrance is to the east of the pier; a stream accompanied by rising steam flows out of the cave into the pond. There is a stack of crates with three food sacks to the right of the entrance, and several [Nordic barnacle clusters](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle_Cluster "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle Cluster") on the rock walls on either side of the entrance. A [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") is a short distance east of the cave, with an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") slightly northwest of that.

### Stony Creek Cave

Stony Creek Cave interior

The cave itself consists of the stream that fills the pond at the entrance, and has two main areas. The first thing you see upon entering is a dead [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") drooped over a beam in front of the stream. The water here contains some [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)") and two lootable [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). The path consists of some planks that extend into the water to the right-hand side of the water. After turning the first corner along the path formed by the stream, the air appears to be shimmering; this is [flammable gas](/wiki/Skyrim:Flammable_Gas "Skyrim:Flammable Gas"), and can be ignited with [flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames") or a torch (just having a fire spell equipped is enough to set it off). The gas extends almost to the final chamber and partway into the side chamber, and if ignited, will deal significant damage to any enemies caught in the blast. However, any remaining enemies will be on high alert after igniting the gas, making any further stealth approach very difficult. The tunnel is patrolled by two bandits.

The side chamber is down a tunnel to the right shortly before the main path takes a left turn. There is a bandit on lookout here on high alert; he is always sitting on the edge of the planks beside a lantern at the entrance to the side tunnel, even though a chair is available for use. At the bottom of the planks is a lootable skeleton, and behind the bandit is a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), an [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), and a [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"). To the left before the fungi and between the lit sconces, the tunnel continues to the side chamber. Halfway through the tunnel is a tripwire which triggers a [swinging mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace") trap hanging from the ceiling, but if you sprint through the trap, the swinging mace should not hit you.

The side chamber contains the boss bandit, who carries [Treasure Map X](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_X "Skyrim:Treasure Map X"). With the [Ruin's Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruin%27s_Edge "Skyrim:Ruin's Edge") Creation installed, the boss will also be carrying the bow [Ruin's Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruin%27s_Edge_(item) "Skyrim:Ruin's Edge (item)") the first time you kill him. The boss chamber also contains an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") with a bowl of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm") on top. To the left of the lab is a table with an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing") and a bowl holding some [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flowers on top. To the right is a bench with an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"), a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), a bowl of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), and the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Mystery of Talara, Part 4](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_Part_4 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, Part 4")*. In the corner is the unlocked boss chest, which contains [Finn's Lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute_(item) "Skyrim:Finn's Lute (item)") and other random loot. Growing around the chamber are two [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), one [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"), and one Namira's rot.

Returning to the tunnel and going north, on a ledge to the right just past the end of the gas is a Namira's rot. There is one last bandit in the large chamber, mining one of the two [moonstone ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein") that are marked by lit lanterns. The chamber also contains an apprentice-locked chest near the ore vein to the left, a couple more skeletons that can be looted, and several food sacks. With the [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") Creation installed, a unique [Bliss Bug in a Jar](/wiki/Skyrim:Bliss_Bug_in_a_Jar "Skyrim:Bliss Bug in a Jar") is on a pair of crates immediately to the left as you enter the chamber. Finally, a waterfall falls from a ledge on the rear wall, with an exit from [Kagrenzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrenzel "Skyrim:Kagrenzel") in the short tunnel beyond. This exit is accessible from this direction by carefully jumping up the small rock face beneath the waterfall or by using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") when standing on a small hill to the right of the waterfall.

## Notes

- Stony Creek Cave also [appears](/wiki/Legends:Eastmarch_Camp "Legends:Eastmarch Camp") in *[Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends")*.
- You can enter [Kagrenzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrenzel "Skyrim:Kagrenzel") from Stony Creek Cave by carefully jumping up the small rock face beneath the waterfall at the end of the cave or by using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") shout when standing on a small hill to the right of the waterfall. However, the room with the glowing orb in Kagrenzel is not normally accessible if you enter from this direction.

## Bugs

- For quests related to Kagrenzel, your map marker may point you to Stony Creek Cave. This also applies to the [Clairvoyance](/wiki/Skyrim:Clairvoyance_(spell) "Skyrim:Clairvoyance (spell)") spell.
- It is advised not to take Finn's Lute until the quest [Finn's Lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute "Skyrim:Finn's Lute") has been started, as it will not be removed from your inventory if taken beforehand.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.5, fixes this bug.
- The chief bandit carrying the treasure map may not appear. Forcing the dungeon to respawn, either through starting one of the quests that require a boss bandit or waiting 30 days, should make the boss spawn. **?**

# Skyrim:Storm Mage

## Overview

**Storm Mages** are enemy spellcasters who specialize in the [Shock Damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Shock_Damage "Skyrim:Shock Damage") branch of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). Like other elemental mages ([fire mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Mage "Skyrim:Fire Mage") and [ice mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage")), they belong to the [Fire/Frost/Shock Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock_Mage "Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock Mage") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of storm mage you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level storm mages even at high levels, but boss-level storm mages will always be at the highest possible level.

### Storm Mages

A powerful Arch Electromancer fires a bolt of lightning

Storm mages rely on powerful shock-based spells in combat, and carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Clothing") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, storm mages have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in the mages' inventories in-game is set at 0%.

On death, storm mages have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

The lowest level storm mages (Novice Storm Mages) do not have any miscellaneous items; they are equipped only with the boots, robes, and daggers listed above.

Electromancers and Arch Electromancers have the same gear as lower-level storm mages, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Staff of Chain Lightning") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

### Storm Mage Bosses

An Apprentice Storm Mage charges a shock spell

Apprentice Storm Mage bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level storm mages listed above. Storm Mage Adepts, Storm Mages, Storm Wizards and Electromancer bosses have the same inventory as the Electromancer and Arch Electromancer listed above, with the exception that Storm Mage Adepts and Storm Mages have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Lightning Bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Lightning_Bolts "Skyrim:Staff of Lightning Bolts") rather than a Staff of Chain Lightning.

| [Haldyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Haldyn "Skyrim:Haldyn") | [Japhet's Folly Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet%27s_Folly_Towers "Skyrim:Japhet's Folly Towers") | The Redguard leader of some pirates called The Blood Horkers |
| [Kornalus](/wiki/Skyrim:Kornalus "Skyrim:Kornalus") | [Harmugstahl](/wiki/Skyrim:Harmugstahl "Skyrim:Harmugstahl") | An Altmer conducting experiments on [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") |
| [Ma'randru-jo](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27randru-jo "Skyrim:Ma'randru-jo") | Outside [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") or [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | A somewhat brusque Khajiit travelling with [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad"), [Atahbah](/wiki/Skyrim:Atahbah "Skyrim:Atahbah"), and [Khayla](/wiki/Skyrim:Khayla "Skyrim:Khayla") in a [trade caravan](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") |
| [Orthorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthorn "Skyrim:Orthorn") | [Fellglow Keep Dungeons](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep_Dungeons "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep Dungeons") | A former apprentice from the College of Winterhold who stole some [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books") when he left |
| [Thorek](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorek "Skyrim:Thorek") | [Nightcaller Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightcaller_Temple "Skyrim:Nightcaller Temple") | A Nord worshipper of [Vaermina](/wiki/Skyrim:Vaermina "Skyrim:Vaermina") guarding the [Skull of Corruption](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull_of_Corruption "Skyrim:Skull of Corruption") |
| [Veren Duleri](/wiki/Skyrim:Veren_Duleri "Skyrim:Veren Duleri") | Nightcaller Temple | A Dunmer worshipper of Vaermina guarding the Skull of Corruption |

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Notes

- All the generic shock mages that are High Elves are listed twice in the leveled lists, which means shock mages are slightly more likely to be High Elves than one of the other races.

# Skyrim:Storm Mage

## Overview

**Storm Mages** are enemy spellcasters who specialize in the [Shock Damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Shock_Damage "Skyrim:Shock Damage") branch of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). Like other elemental mages ([fire mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Mage "Skyrim:Fire Mage") and [ice mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage")), they belong to the [Fire/Frost/Shock Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock_Mage "Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock Mage") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of storm mage you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level storm mages even at high levels, but boss-level storm mages will always be at the highest possible level.

### Storm Mages

A powerful Arch Electromancer fires a bolt of lightning

Storm mages rely on powerful shock-based spells in combat, and carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Clothing") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, storm mages have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in the mages' inventories in-game is set at 0%.

On death, storm mages have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

The lowest level storm mages (Novice Storm Mages) do not have any miscellaneous items; they are equipped only with the boots, robes, and daggers listed above.

Electromancers and Arch Electromancers have the same gear as lower-level storm mages, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Staff of Chain Lightning") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

### Storm Mage Bosses

An Apprentice Storm Mage charges a shock spell

Apprentice Storm Mage bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level storm mages listed above. Storm Mage Adepts, Storm Mages, Storm Wizards and Electromancer bosses have the same inventory as the Electromancer and Arch Electromancer listed above, with the exception that Storm Mage Adepts and Storm Mages have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Lightning Bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Lightning_Bolts "Skyrim:Staff of Lightning Bolts") rather than a Staff of Chain Lightning.

## Named Storm Mages

A Storm Mage Adept

| Name | Location | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano") | [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements") | A representative of the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") serving as an advisor at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") |
| [Aranea Ienith](/wiki/Skyrim:Aranea_Ienith "Skyrim:Aranea Ienith") | [Shrine of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Azura "Skyrim:Shrine of Azura") | A worshipper of [Azura](/wiki/Lore:Azura "Lore:Azura") who will help you find and cleanse [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star") |
| [Ardwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Ardwen "Skyrim:Ardwen") | Wilderness | A pilgrim on her way to see the restored [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") (can also be an [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") or [fire mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Mage "Skyrim:Fire Mage")) |
| [The Caller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Caller "Skyrim:The Caller") | [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep") | The elemental mage leader of the mages found in the keep (can also be an [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") or [fire mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Mage "Skyrim:Fire Mage")) |
| [Drelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas "Skyrim:Drelas") | [Drelas' Cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas%27_Cottage "Skyrim:Drelas' Cottage") | A hostile elemental mage living south of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") (can also be an [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") or [fire mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Mage "Skyrim:Fire Mage")) |
| [Estormo](/wiki/Skyrim:Estormo "Skyrim:Estormo") | [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") | A Thalmor agent working for Ancano |

| [Ma'randru-jo](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27randru-jo "Skyrim:Ma'randru-jo") | Outside [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") or [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | A somewhat brusque Khajiit travelling with [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad"), [Atahbah](/wiki/Skyrim:Atahbah "Skyrim:Atahbah"), and [Khayla](/wiki/Skyrim:Khayla "Skyrim:Khayla") in a [trade caravan](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") |
| [Orthorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthorn "Skyrim:Orthorn") | [Fellglow Keep Dungeons](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep_Dungeons "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep Dungeons") | A former apprentice from the College of Winterhold who stole some [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books") when he left |
| [Thorek](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorek "Skyrim:Thorek") | [Nightcaller Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightcaller_Temple "Skyrim:Nightcaller Temple") | A Nord worshipper of [Vaermina](/wiki/Skyrim:Vaermina "Skyrim:Vaermina") guarding the [Skull of Corruption](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull_of_Corruption "Skyrim:Skull of Corruption") |
| [Veren Duleri](/wiki/Skyrim:Veren_Duleri "Skyrim:Veren Duleri") | Nightcaller Temple | A Dunmer worshipper of Vaermina guarding the Skull of Corruption |

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Notes

- All the generic shock mages that are High Elves are listed twice in the leveled lists, which means shock mages are slightly more likely to be High Elves than one of the other races.

# Skyrim:Storm Mage

## Overview

**Storm Mages** are enemy spellcasters who specialize in the [Shock Damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Shock_Damage "Skyrim:Shock Damage") branch of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). Like other elemental mages ([fire mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Mage "Skyrim:Fire Mage") and [ice mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage")), they belong to the [Fire/Frost/Shock Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock_Mage "Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock Mage") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of storm mage you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level storm mages even at high levels, but boss-level storm mages will always be at the highest possible level.

### Storm Mages

A powerful Arch Electromancer fires a bolt of lightning

Storm mages rely on powerful shock-based spells in combat, and carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Clothing") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, storm mages have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in the mages' inventories in-game is set at 0%.

On death, storm mages have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

The lowest level storm mages (Novice Storm Mages) do not have any miscellaneous items; they are equipped only with the boots, robes, and daggers listed above.

Electromancers and Arch Electromancers have the same gear as lower-level storm mages, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Staff of Chain Lightning") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

### Storm Mage Bosses

An Apprentice Storm Mage charges a shock spell

Apprentice Storm Mage bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level storm mages listed above. Storm Mage Adepts, Storm Mages, Storm Wizards and Electromancer bosses have the same inventory as the Electromancer and Arch Electromancer listed above, with the exception that Storm Mage Adepts and Storm Mages have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Lightning Bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Lightning_Bolts "Skyrim:Staff of Lightning Bolts") rather than a Staff of Chain Lightning.
