| [Veren Duleri](/wiki/Skyrim:Veren_Duleri "Skyrim:Veren Duleri") | Nightcaller Temple | A Dunmer worshipper of Vaermina guarding the Skull of Corruption |

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Notes

- All the generic shock mages that are High Elves are listed twice in the leveled lists, which means shock mages are slightly more likely to be High Elves than one of the other races.

# Skyrim:Striking the Heart

## Overview

## Radiant Options

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Aela](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress") in Whiterun.
2. Travel to the designated hideout.
3. Kill the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand") leader.
4. Return to Aela.

## Detailed Walkthrough

At the end of [The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand"), you and [Aela](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress") discover [Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor") dead on the ground. You and Aela start your own personal vendetta by assassinating a Silver Hand leader at a radiant location.

All of the radiant locations contain good loot. See the appropriate location's page, listed above, to find out where the loot is. There are a lot of Silver Hand, though, and the leader is often a lot harder to kill. Once the leader is dead (explore the location like you would in a regular dungeon or camp) return to Aela in [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr"), and she will give you leveled gold and start the next quest, either [Retrieval](/wiki/Skyrim:Retrieval "Skyrim:Retrieval") or [Stealing Plans](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealing_Plans "Skyrim:Stealing Plans").

### Reward

| Levels[†](#intnote_LevelNote) | Reward[‡](#intnote_RewardBug) | USLEEP Reward |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 100 | 100 |
| 10–19 | 150 | 150 |
| 20–29 | 300 | 200 |
| 30–39 | 300 | 250 |
| 40+ | 300 | 300 |

[†](#note_LevelNote)Level is based on when the player completed the previous quest (or level one for the first quest), not the player's level when receiving the quest or its reward.

[‡](#note_RewardBug)The reward amounts for radiant Companions quests do not progress as intended.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=20007))

## Bugs

- This quest uses the Radiant Quest System to randomly generate a target location and waypoint for the objectives. In some cases the waypoint will lead to a random spot adjacent to the designated quest location. This is caused when you have previously killed the Silver Hand leader.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.6, fixes this bug.
- If the quest is given but no waypoint is provided, and killing all NPCs at given location does nothing, the quest is most likely not activated.
  - To see if any quest is active, type **showquesttargets** in the console in-game. Look for 'CR09', the ID for this quest.
  - If not there, yet the quest is clearly in your quest tab, the quest can be completed by simply writing **completequest cr09** in the console in-game.
  - The quest completion should pop up, and returning to Aela should give you the follow-up quest in the Companion quest chain.
- After returning and reporting to Aela, your quest will be acknowledged as complete in the journal, but it may remain in your active quest list. If this happens, Aela will not give you any further Silver Hand radiant quest to do (but will still give [Skyrim:Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination "Skyrim:Animal Extermination") quests). This bug can occurr with any Silver Hand radiant quest. **?** Confirmed=1

## Quest Stages

| Striking the Heart (CR09) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | We've heard rumors of a Silver Hand lieutenant camped at <Alias=Camp>. With <Alias.PronounObj=CampBoss> dead, their forces should weaken. *Objective 10:* Assassinate the Silver Hand leader |
| 20 |  | I killed the Silver Hand leader at <Alias=Camp>. *Objective 20:* Return to Aela |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 100.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CR09 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CR09`.

# Skyrim:Summerset Shadows

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. |  |  |

| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Remove a rival guild from the picture.** |

|  |  |

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | Five [Thieves Guild Special Jobs](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Special_Job_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") in Windhelm | | |

The banner of the Summerset Shadows in Uttering Hills Cave

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
2. Find out the mission details from [Torsten Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Torsten_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Torsten Cruel-Sea") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").
3. Speak to [Niranye](/wiki/Skyrim:Niranye "Skyrim:Niranye").
4. Travel to [Uttering Hills Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Uttering_Hills_Cave "Skyrim:Uttering Hills Cave").
5. Recover [Fjotli's Silver Locket](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotli%27s_Silver_Locket "Skyrim:Fjotli's Silver Locket").
6. Return to [Torsten Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Torsten_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Torsten Cruel-Sea").

### A Special Job

Once you've completed five additional jobs in the city of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), speak to Delvin at the Ragged Flagon to receive a 'special job'. Delvin explains that he has received word from a friend in Windhelm of a rival faction of thieves setting up shop. Travel to Windhelm and speak to Torsten Cruel-Sea. He can be found wandering both inside and outside the city walls. Talk to Torsten, and he'll tell you that the faction killed his daughter and stole her silver locket. He has already tracked down her killer and dealt swift justice, but not before learning about the formation of a new, rival Guild. Torsten wants the locket back and revenge on the people behind the murder. He'll give you a name, [Niranye](/wiki/Skyrim:Niranye "Skyrim:Niranye"), that he prised from the murderer before killing him. She is somewhere in Windhelm.

### An Old Friend, Working for the Enemy

During the day, Niranye is usually at her stall near [The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(place) "Skyrim:The White Phial (place)"). In the evening, she can often be found in the [New Gnisis Cornerclub](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub"). Talk to her about Torsten's daughter and she'll express her sympathy over the tragedy of Fjotli's murder. To persuade Niranye to tell the truth, you must pass a [hard speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Hard "Skyrim:Speech").

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| You might be a decent thief, but you're an awful actor. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Now, just a moment. Let's think about this... you know, discuss it like two rational people. **Failed**: I'm afraid I have absolutely no idea what you're speaking of. | | | | **Passed**: Locate the hideout **Failed**: Nothing |
| Tell me everything or end up like Fjotli! **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Now, just a moment. Let's think about this... you know, discuss it like two rational people. **Failed**: Now you're threatening me? What in the name of the Divines is wrong with you? | | | | **Passed**: Locate the hideout **Failed**: Nothing |
| I don't have time for this! | Think I'm defenseless? Well you're wrong! | | | | Turn hostile |
| My mistake. | Next time you wish to accuse someone of a crime, I suggest you obtain proof! | | | | Nothing |

If you cannot convince her to tell the truth, you have two options to proceed. The first option is confronting her with evidence to get her to talk. The proof is in Niranye's house, on the east side of Windhelm. There is a hidden panel to the rear of the eastern room, which leads to the basement. In the safe to the right of the shelves are the *[first](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Letter_from_Linwe "Skyrim:First Letter from Linwe")* and *[second](/wiki/Skyrim:Second_Letter_from_Linwe "Skyrim:Second Letter from Linwe")* letters from [Linwe](/wiki/Skyrim:Linwe "Skyrim:Linwe"), the Summerset Shadows leader. The second option is to tell her you've "had enough of this" (one of the dialogue choices). At this point, she becomes hostile, allowing you to kill her without accruing a bounty--nearby NPCs will even help you. You can then loot the letter from Linwe off her corpse. However, if kept alive, she becomes a fence after completing this quest, so the first option may be preferable.

Either way reveals that the rival guild were not responsible for Fjotli's death, merely that they looted her body, and that their hideout is in [Uttering Hills Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Uttering_Hills_Cave "Skyrim:Uttering Hills Cave").

### Send a Message

The burning banner

[Uttering Hills Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Uttering_Hills_Cave "Skyrim:Uttering Hills Cave") is in the mountains to the west of Windhelm. Travel there, and either sneak past or kill the [Summerset Shadow](/wiki/Skyrim:Summerset_Shadow "Skyrim:Summerset Shadow") lookouts outside. None of the generic Shadows can be looted for their armor. Inside, on the small table is a leveled poison; when the path splits there is a single Shadow patrolling each tunnel and both paths lead to the same cave. There are two Shadows warming themselves by a fire with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), there is a chest beside the fire, and a [Corundum Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") vein to the west.

The door leads to a circular tower room; at the bottom there is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and a random potion. Hanging above the lab is a dried [Elves Ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a dried [Frost Mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). A bandit patrols between the room and the next stairs, and another one is sitting at the far end of the tunnel. There is an adept-level chest on the other side of the wall that the lab is on. The room to the right contains the Summerset Shadows banner, and when approached will give you the option of burning it, which can be done using a fire spell. Doing so will alert any remaining enemies, so leave it until after they are dead if you want to remain hidden.

There is a door to either side of the banner. The room to the left contains two Shadows, one awake and one sleeping, a knapsack, and a leveled potion. The other room contains the Shadows' boss, Linwe, a bed to the left, the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") skill book *[Mace Etiquette](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace_Etiquette "Skyrim:Mace Etiquette")* on the shelves opposite the end of the bed, and a boss chest to the right.

Linwe is instantly hostile to you and, when dead, you can loot his body for the locket, some leveled weapons, and his [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Linwe%27s_Armor "Skyrim:Linwe's Armor"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Linwe%27s_Boots "Skyrim:Linwe's Boots"), [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Linwe%27s_Gloves "Skyrim:Linwe's Gloves") and [hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Linwe%27s_Hood "Skyrim:Linwe's Hood"). There is no quick way out so you must retrace your steps back outside and return to Torsten.

Alternatively you can sneak all the way to Linwe and steal the Locket, staying true to the Thieves Guild code of not killing its targets, though you should be warned that Linwe has a *very* high detection level. After taking the locket, the quest updates as if Linwe had been killed. The game still reports the Summerset Shadows as being overthrown, even if you haven't killed anyone.
Burning the banner is still possible if you have a high sneak perk. Distract Linwe and the other Summerset Shadows to stay at a distance while you burn it, and hide immediately after.

### Message Delivered

Return to Torsten in Windhelm and return his heirloom. He'll reward you with a leveled item, and offer his support to the Guild.

Report back to Delvin. He'll give you your pay, and will compliment you on your actions and point out that the added infamy you earned the guild has attracted a new merchant to [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon").

## Notes

- In the future, you may be attacked by a Summerset Shadow, presumably in revenge.
- After completing this quest, three [Thief Cache](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_Cache "Skyrim:Thief Cache") barrels will appear around Windhelm.
- The banner can also be burnt by attacking it with a weapon (either ranged or melee) that has been enchanted with fire damage. Torches, on the other hand, can't be used to set the banner on fire.

## Bugs

- The Summerset Shadows Banner may not render properly. You will see a quest arrow marking an empty spot between two pillars. Aim your fire at the location and you will still destroy the banner.
- The banner looks normal when it is intact, but disappears once it is set on fire. This does not affect the quest in any way. The problem can be solved by first saving, then loading a save in a different area, and finally loading the Uttering Hills Cave save.
- The optional objective to burn the banner sometimes doesn't pop up. This appears to occur if you kill Linwe before approaching the banner.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.
  - The banner may still be burned.
- Once Summerset Shadows has been completed, Uttering Hills Cave will no longer be populated by bandits but with respawning members of the Summerset Shadows. This can be a potential problem if the player has not completed quests that may require this location, such as [killing Bandit leaders](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
  -  To fix this issue, use the console commands `prid c5675`, followed by `disable`.
- After accepting the quest it may not start and won't be present in the quest journal. Talking to Delvin again does not solve this, making the [Thieves Guild's](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") upgrade quest line broken. **?**
  - Talking directly to Torsten Cruel-Sea may continue the quest as usual.
  -  You can get the quest started by using the console command `setstage tgtq04 0`.
- Burning the banner may cause the game to freeze. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Summerset Shadows (TGTQ04) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Torsten Cruel-Sea, a wealthy merchant residing in Windhelm, has requested assistance from the Thieves Guild. *Objective 10:* Speak to Torsten Cruel-Sea |
| 20 |  | Torsten Cruel-Sea's daughter Fjotli was slain and robbed of a silver locket by a Thieves Guild hailing from Summerset Isle. Calling themselves "The Summerset Shadows," they are looking into expanding their influence in Skyrim. *Objective 20:* Speak to Niranye |
| 25 |  | *Objective 30:* (Optional) Discover leverage to sway Niranye |
| 40 |  | Torsten's daughter wasn't slain by the Summerset Shadows, but their leader, Linwe, has them robbing the dead of their valuables. Linwe and the rest of his guild have established a hideout in Uttering Hills Cave. *Objective 40:* Travel to Uttering Hills Cave |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Recover Fjolti's *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* Silver Locket |
| 55 |  | *Objective 60:* (Optional) Destroy the Summerset Shadow's Banner |
| 60 |  | I've slain Linwe and obtained Fjotli's Silver Locket. This ends the presence of the Summerset Shadows in Skyrim. *Objective 70:* Return to Torsten Cruel-Sea |
| 200 | ☑ | The locket has been returned to Torsten Cruel-Sea, and the Thieves Guild can now count on him as an influential ally in Windhelm. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 30, 35, 65.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGTQ04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGTQ04`.

# Skyrim:Summoning Karstaag

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Summon and defeat [Karstaag](/wiki/Skyrim:Karstaag "Skyrim:Karstaag").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | [Glacial Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Glacial_Cave "Skyrim:Glacial Cave"), [Castle Karstaag Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Ruins "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Ruins") |
| Reward: | [Summon Karstaag](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Karstaag "Skyrim:Summon Karstaag") power |
| ID: | DLC2dunKarstaagQST |

Karstaag summoned and hostile

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note**: This quest does not appear in your journal.

1. Travel to the [Glacial Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Glacial_Cave "Skyrim:Glacial Cave").
2. Retrieve [Karstaag's skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Karstaag%27s_Skull "Skyrim:Karstaag's Skull") from the back wall of the cave.
3. Travel to [Castle Karstaag](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Ruins "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Ruins").
4. Make your way through the [Castle Karstaag Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Caverns "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Caverns") or pick the lock on the front door.
5. Place Karstaag's skull on his throne.
6. Kill [Karstaag](/wiki/Skyrim:Karstaag "Skyrim:Karstaag").

## Detailed Walkthrough

Karstaag's skull in Glacial Cave

Karstaag's skull placed on his throne

The [Glacial Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Glacial_Cave "Skyrim:Glacial Cave") is very simple, containing only three [Rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling"). [Karstaag's skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Karstaag%27s_Skull "Skyrim:Karstaag's Skull") is in the wall at the very back of the cave with torches around it.

After traveling to the [ruins of Castle Karstaag](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Ruins "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Ruins"), there are two ways to reach the courtyard: You can either pick the master-level lock on the front gate, or take the long route through the [Castle Karstaag Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Caverns "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Caverns"), a large Riekling cave. The cave crisscrosses the main cavern multiple times and there are Rieklings on every level.

Once you get to the courtyard, you will see a large throne. Place the skull here. Be prepared for a very difficult fight. Once you place the skull, back up. [Karstaag](/wiki/Skyrim:Karstaag "Skyrim:Karstaag") will appear as a ghostly frost giant with horns and a permanent ice cloak. When he appears he will cause a massive explosion of ice that looks like a blizzard which will hang around a while and take up a large area. Karstaag fights like a regular [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") but hits a lot harder. He can summon three [ice wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith") at any time in the fight and he can do it multiple times. He is a very powerful foe and can kill poorly-equipped characters rapidly.

When you defeat Karstaag, you will gain the power to [Summon Karstaag](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Karstaag "Skyrim:Summon Karstaag"), but only three times and only outside. You can also loot Karstaag for ten samples of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm") and a few [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems").

## Notes

- It is possible to summon Karstaag, leave using the front door, and then climb over the ice wall (just to the right of the door, while looking at the door) to strike at him from above. He and his summons will not be able to strike the player while standing on the ice above. Karstaag will move towards the door in pursuit of the player but he never actually exits, making him an easy long distance target. Player summons and companions will still attempt to fight Karstaag on ground level.
- It's possible for Karstaag to knock you back into the [Castle Karstaag Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Caverns "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Caverns"), resetting the fight, and thus his health.

## Quest Stages

- All of the quest stages are empty: 0, 10, 20, 30, 240, 250, 255.

# Skyrim:Sun Stone

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Standing Stones.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Standing_Stones.png) | All-Maker Stone: Sun Stone ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Sun+Stone)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 10 |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2StoneSun | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| North-northwest of [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)") West-southwest of [Nchardak](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchardak "Skyrim:Nchardak") | |

The Sun Stone

The **Sun Stone** is an [All-Maker Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:All-Maker_Stones "Skyrim:All-Maker Stones") north-northwest of [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)").

Once [cleansed](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones"), this stone gives you the power to cause a [Sun Flare](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Flare "Skyrim:Sun Flare"), a fiery explosion that deals up to 100 points of fire damage around you, with greater damage done within this range to closer enemies. Once you use this power, it disappears from the Powers menu, and you must return to the Sun Stone to obtain it again.

## Related Quests

- **[Cleansing the Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones")**: Use the [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") to cleanse each of the remaining [All-Maker Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:All-Maker_Stones "Skyrim:All-Maker Stones").

## Walkthrough

The stone shows the usual signs of construction, with wooden scaffolding on the west side, and [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), [shovels](/wiki/Skyrim:Shovel "Skyrim:Shovel"), hammers, and carts in the vicinity. Several [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") plants and [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungi grow around the stone. A path leads south to Tel Mithryn.

Before you cleanse the stone, during the day, six [unique reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver#Temple_and_Pillar_Workers "Skyrim:Reaver") will be working on and bowing to the stone. During the night, [Drovas Relvi](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi"), [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren"), and [Ulves Romoran](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulves_Romoran "Skyrim:Ulves Romoran") will also be found at the stone. When you cleanse the stone, a leveled [lurker](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker") will rise from the water around the base of the stone and attack you and the workers. After the lurker is defeated, the reavers will remain peaceful and be removed from the game once you leave the area, and the other workers will express their thanks and return to Tel Mithryn.

## Notes

- The Sun Stone also appears in *[Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Sun_Stone "Bloodmoon:Sun Stone")*.

## Bugs

- If [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") is finished and this Stone has been cleansed, [Drovas Relvi](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi")'s sleep package will always be active, and therefore he will be found sleeping indefinitely in [Tel Mithryn Steward's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Steward%27s_House "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Steward's House").
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.
- If Reluctant Steward is finished and this Stone has been cleansed, Drovas Relvi's sleep package may still have him trying to sleep at the [Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch"), even though he won't work there anymore.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Sundered Towers

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Tower.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Tower.png) | Nordic Tower: Sundered Towers ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sundered+Towers)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Sundered_Towers "Lore:Sundered Towers")) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No (see [Notes](#Notes)) |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Occupants | |
| [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), [Hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| RedEagleRedoubtExterior08 | |
| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| Southeast of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") Northeast of [Red Eagle Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Redoubt "Skyrim:Red Eagle Redoubt") | |

Sundered Towers

**Sundered Towers** is a small pair of linked ruined [Nordic towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") southeast of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") and [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven").

## Related Quests

- **[Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)")**: Find [Red Eagle's](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle "Skyrim:Red Eagle") [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Bane").

## Walkthrough

The towers are at the top of a series of stone staircases and winding paths interspersed with landings occupied by the Forsworn camped at [Red Eagle Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Redoubt "Skyrim:Red Eagle Redoubt"). The entrance to the towers is a level-locked iron door which can be unlocked with the [Red Eagle Tower key](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Tower_Key "Skyrim:Red Eagle Tower Key") carried by the Forsworn Briarheart of the redoubt. Inside is a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* and a random pair of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets") on a sideboard opposite. A flight of stairs to the right ascends to a doorway outside to a wooden ramp up to the next level, where a raised wooden bridge is on the right and a doorway is to the left. Just inside on the right is a chain that lowers the bridge. At the back of the room behind a flight of wooden stairs is an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"), while the stairs lead up to another level with more stairs up to the highest level; both of these levels are empty.

Once you have lowered the wooden bridge, you may cross to a second tower to the east. On the far side is a doorway ahead and a wooden ramp down to the left. Through the door, the room contains a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a flight of wooden stairs leading up, with another flight above these leading to the top; again, these levels are both empty. Descending via the ramp brings you to a doorway with a broken sideboard opposite holding a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") and a random empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). There are also stairs leading down on the right as you enter. At the bottom is a pile of rubble with a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") among it, with an iron door opposite secured by a bar on this side preventing entrance from the other side.

## Notes

- This location cannot be independently [cleared](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons"). It will only show up as such when the boss-level creatures in Red Eagle Redoubt have been killed, as the game considers these zones one unit for the purpose of calculating clears.
  - Sundered Towers itself will never add to your count of cleared locations, and therefore does not contribute to the [Delver](/wiki/Skyrim:Delver "Skyrim:Delver") achievement.
- Although the door bar prevents easy access to Sundered Towers from the plateau, this can be circumvented by climbing a rock ramp opposite the third tree south of the barred door, then jumping up more rocks to reach the tower with the bridge release chain. This approach allows [Red Eagle Ascent](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Redoubt#Red_Eagle_Ascent "Skyrim:Red Eagle Redoubt") to be traversed downward instead of upward.

## Bugs

- The key might not be on the corpse of the Briarheart.
- The book may clip through the pillar on the altar, making it irretrievable. **?**
  - Cast an explosive area-of-effect spell such as [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball"), and the book should reveal itself, allowing you to grab it.
- Killing and looting the Briarheart may fail to complete the corresponding quest objective for [Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial"). **?**
  - Kill and loot the Briarheart before talking to [Quintus Navale](/wiki/Skyrim:Quintus_Navale "Skyrim:Quintus Navale"), which should mark the quest objective as complete. Then, return to Quintus and proceed with the quest.

# Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge

## Overview

Sunderstone Gorge

**Sunderstone Gorge** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north-northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). It contains only one zone, *[Sunderstone Gorge](#Sunderstone_Gorge)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret.
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave.
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir").
- **[Hunting the Monster](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_the_Monster "Skyrim:Hunting the Monster")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Destroy the [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") target.

### Exterior

Two sets of skeletal remains and blood splashed cairns lead up to the gorge's mountain entrance. A single, leveled [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") is found standing beside the entrance and will try to bar your entry. They can be very hard to spot from any distance as they blend in very well.

### Sunderstone Gorge

Once inside the path leads downward to the first of many [pressure plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers a [falling boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") trap. It is best to avoid this trap, as setting it off carries you, along with the boulders, down past some skeletal remains and over to a necromancer sitting by a fire. There are three pieces of firewood beside the fire. By avoiding the trap, you have the elevated advantage for a ranged attack on the mage. At the bottom of the path the gorge turns eastward into a narrow passage.

The second trap

The passage opens up into a space with a second pressure plate that triggers a [swinging mammoth skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Skull_Ram "Skyrim:Traps") trap. A skeleton patrols the small cavity occupied by the trap. The crevice through which you pass into this area is narrow, so activating the plate from a distance with [Magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Magelight "Skyrim:Magelight") or a ranged shot with a bow can trigger the ram, allowing safe clearance and dealing with the skeleton simultaneously. Another possibility is to touch the plate and quickly jump backward into the safety of the narrow passage, though if your follower is too close behind you this could be disastrous. A random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") can be found on a small ledge just behind the mammoth skull, on the east wall. The path continues through a narrow passage on the south wall. Watch for the [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") which may alert enemies lurking farther along.

A skeleton waits around the right corner in the next room. Before entering, note the pressure plate next to the left corner of the opening next to an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick"). This triggers a [flame spout trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap"). Safely igniting the slick from your position in the passage will clear the low-level enemies within. A [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") is on the eastern wall to the right of a side passage. In this passage is a ledge used as a shortcut exit later. Here you will find an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") and three additional silver ore veins, one on the right and two on the left walls, with a [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") lurking between them. The main path continues north through a crevice revealing the open sky above, with water raining down into the pathway feeding the plentiful [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") you can harvest along the way.

Oil lanterns everywhere

Note where the oil slick on the floor begins again and the numerous [oil lanterns](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") hanging from above. A necromancer, a skeleton, and two [fire mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Mage "Skyrim:Fire Mage") await on the raised platform and in the clearing ahead. You can use the oil and lanterns for a preemptive strike; however, this alerts all enemies to your presence and location. A pressure plate triggering a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") is at the mouth of the clearing, just below the raised platform. Avoid it, or make use of it during battle. Opposite this, against the wall is an open crate containing a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") and two potatoes. Beside the crate sits a barrel with a hammer, a lantern, a bottle of ale, and a coin purse. When the area is clear, a small room to the right contains an adept-locked chest. There is nothing of note in the area behind the spike wall, so continue up the two ramps to a landing. On the landing look directly ahead, to the south, for a bucket on the ground. Behind the bucket, tucked into a niche, is an apprentice-locked chest. Follow the bridge across the room, heading east to an intersection. Take a left at the intersection to find a wooden door leading to the next room along the eastern wall.

The doors open to the living quarters where a fire mage and a leveled [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") are waiting. Another oil slick is on the floor if you wish to make use of it. A [spellcaster trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellcaster_Trap "Skyrim:Spellcaster Trap") shooting flames is immediately to the right before the room opens up. Dodge the flames and remove the [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") to disable the trap. Three [spider eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg") are found in a broken urn to the left of the first pillar, with an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing") in a second broken urn along with a large stone pot against the same wall. On the right side of the room, just past the soul gem trap, a wooden door opens to a storage room. Opening the door will trigger a [poison dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") unless the adept-locked tension cable is first disarmed. The darts are easy to avoid by standing to the far left of the door and then opening it. Inside is a shelf with a random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") and a chest. Next to the storage room is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"). A number of ingredients and a potion are on the table with the lab, but may have been flung about in the skirmish. On the table, or around it on the floor, find a potion, three bunches of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries"), a bowl of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), a piece of [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root") and a bowl of [moon sugar](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Sugar "Skyrim:Moon Sugar"). Farther in the room are three holding cells containing nothing of interest. Across from the cells, the room opens up into the living quarters. On the dresser by the two beds find some loose septims and a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower. A [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") and a shelf with a mage's robe are against the wall. In the alcove at the far end of the room, nestled in the rubble is a master-locked chest. To the left is a plinth with a random helmet and to the right is the narrow trail leading onward.

The word wall

The trail takes you to an iron door that opens to a large room with two fire mages on the dais. A [flame atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Flame Atronach") will join in the fray when you enter the room. Battle your way up the stairs to the word wall with a part of the Fire Breath shout (see [bugs](#Bugs)). In front of the wall is a bier with the body of a [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf_(dead) "Skyrim:Wood Elf (dead)"), a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_(dead) "Skyrim:Redguard (dead)"), and an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"). To the right is the boss chest, an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), an urn, and two small [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"). In the center of the platform a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Frostfall, v10](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Frostfall,_v10 "Skyrim:2920, Frostfall, v10")* is on a plinth with a random soul gem on stands, on either side. A bowl of fire salts and a random potion are on the embalming table on the way out. Activate the chain to the left of the portcullis to access the next room. The small work area is lined with shelves. The first shelf to the left holds a bowl of [vampire dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust") and an amethyst. The next shelf holds a [scroll of fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fireball "Skyrim:Scroll of Fireball"), a [scroll of conjure familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Familiar "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Familiar"), and a [scroll of cure wounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Cure_Wounds "Skyrim:Scroll of Cure Wounds"), along with a garnet. On the other side of the room is an alchemy lab, with a potion, a bowl of fire salts, a sample of [creep cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster"), and a piece of canis root. Next is an urn and then a set of shelves with a cast iron pot. Looking inside the pot you will find a sample of [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen") and a [human heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Heart "Skyrim:Human Heart"). The pull chain to exit is next to the urn. The path out takes you to the short side passage you visited previously, only now you are on the stone wall looking down. On the far wall, above the giant stone face, there is a coin purse that you can shoot down, use [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis"), or use an area effect spell to dislodge. Once you have it, jump down and backtrack to exit the gorge.

## Notes

- In addition to the frequent patches of oil throughout the dungeon, there is a circle of oil before the stairs leading up into the room with the final chest. As you approach it, a flame atronach will be summoned through a portal. The atronach can ignite the oil slick; the resulting explosion will damage and possibly kill the atronach.
- The campfire after the rock trap has damaging flames, similar to those found around [Yisra](/wiki/Skyrim:Yisra "Skyrim:Yisra")'s corpse. They will damage anyone who stands in them, be it you, a follower, or the hostile mage tending the fire.

## Bugs

- This location is referred to as "Greywater Gorge" in game letters and your quest journal.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
- At the word wall, you may encounter a bug where the word is absorbed as normal but doesn't appear in the Shouts menu and you cannot unlock it. This is permanent.
  - This may possibly be avoided by approaching the word wall from the left.
- The mage leaning against the wall on the catwalk shortly after the entrance cannot be hit by arrows while in that area.

# Skyrim:Supply and Demand

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [The Silencer](/wiki/User:The_Silencer "User:The Silencer"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [The Silencer](/wiki/User:The_Silencer "User:The Silencer"), *not checked* |

| **Clear [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") for the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").** | |

The Skooma Dealer

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Shipment%27s_Ready "Skyrim:Shipment's Ready") you were required to find to finish the [previous quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Raid "Skyrim:The Raid").
2. Report to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
3. Visit and clear the [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern").
4. Return to the Jarl of Riften.

### Locate The Suppliers

After you have read the [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Shipment%27s_Ready "Skyrim:Shipment's Ready") you will need to return to the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl"). When you tell her that you have discovered the location of the [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") traders, she will ask that they *"be destroyed once and for all"*, and entice you with the prospect of a title in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). This prompts an update of the quest to find the cave.

The cave is north of Riften, and northeast of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"). There is a single [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and two [pit wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Pit_Wolf "Skyrim:Pit Wolf") outside the cave. The wolves should be inside the two level-locked cages, but are sometimes found roaming the small camp.

### Disruption

Cragslane Cavern Guard

The wolf pit of Cragslane Cavern

Enter the cave to find a bandit standing guard near a lit lantern; after you ignore the warnings, or get too close, you will be attacked. Further down the tunnel and around the corner is the main gathering room of the suppliers. There are three [gamblers](/wiki/Skyrim:Gambler "Skyrim:Gambler"), a [barkeep](/wiki/Skyrim:Barkeep "Skyrim:Barkeep"), and a pit wolf in the first part, and a bandit, and two pit wolves locked in cages, in the second part.

Loot the barkeep for the [Craglane chest key](/wiki/Skyrim:Craglane_Chest_Key "Skyrim:Craglane Chest Key"), and the second bandit for the [Craglane dog cage key](/wiki/Skyrim:Craglane_Dog_Cage_Key "Skyrim:Craglane Dog Cage Key"). Go behind the bar in the northwestern corner to find a leveled apprentice-locked chest, a bowl of [moon sugar](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Sugar "Skyrim:Moon Sugar"), two bottles of skooma, and a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Wolf Queen, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v1 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v1")*. The second part of the cave contains another leveled apprentice-locked chest with a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") in front of it, the two apprentice-locked wolf cages, and spread over the preparation area, a few [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), a bowl of moon sugar and seven bottles of skooma. There is also a set of [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes"), which are rare to find lying loose.

### A Reward Well Earned

After two quests involving two fights, one of which descends into a large brawl, you have well earned a reward. Return to the jarl and she will reward you with a random enchanted weapon, and express her gratefulness, *"Your continued efforts have been of great benefit to the people of Riften."*

Additionally, if [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") is jarl, then following the eradication of the bandits in [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern"), she will send her people to gather any remaining merchandise because *"We can't have that substance falling into the wrong hands now, can we?"* She will also reward you with some gold, stating that *"this should suffice as your cut of the... or rather, a reward for your actions."*

## Notes

- Every person in the cave must die for the quest to progress. All the wolves, however, can be spared.
- The rewarded weapon's enchantment and type are both random.
- This is the third of three quests that are required to unlock the option to become [Thane of Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:I_Done_Got_Thaned! "Skyrim:I Done Got Thaned!") for the Jarl of Riften. There are additional requirements noted on that quest's page.

## Bugs

- If [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") has been cleared before receiving the quest, you will need to go to more trouble to complete it.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
  - When this occurs, you need to clear the cavern three times in order for the quest to complete. You need to kill a total of seven bandits to "disrupt the operation", but only the three bandits respawn after you have cleared it. Travel far away and wait thirty days for the cavern to reset. Return and kill the bandits three times to get a total of seven.
  -  You can use the console command `player.setstage FreeformRiften01 40` to advance to the next quest stage.
  -  An alternative workaround is to repeatedly resurrect one of the dead bandits via console until you have a total of seven dead NPCs.
  - Another workaround is to repeatedly resurrect one of the dead bandits via [Dead Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Thrall "Skyrim:Dead Thrall") until you have a total of seven dead NPCs.[*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Supply_and_Demand)*]
- If you exit the cave during the fight and reenter, the quest may not advance.
  - Sometimes after you buy the house the jarl still won't have the quest finishing dialogue.[*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Supply_and_Demand)*]

## Quest Stages

| Supply and Demand (FreeformRiften01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Report skooma source to Jarl of Riften |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Find the skooma dealers in Cragslane Cavern |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Disrupt the skooma operation |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Report to the Jarl of Riften |
| 200 | ☑ | *(Completing quest and starting quest [I Done Got Thaned!](/wiki/Skyrim:I_Done_Got_Thaned! "Skyrim:I Done Got Thaned!"))* |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften01`.

# Skyrim:Surgery

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Alphabetface](/wiki/User:Alphabetface "User:Alphabetface"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Change your appearance.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") |
| Reward: | A new appearance |
| ID: | DLC1Surgery |

*"Beauty or hideous deformity, nothing is beyond my skill."*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. (Optional) Hear rumors about the [Face Sculptor](/wiki/Skyrim:Galathil "Skyrim:Galathil") from an innkeeper or guard.
2. Find [Galathil](/wiki/Skyrim:Galathil "Skyrim:Galathil") in the [Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon").
3. Pay her to change your appearance.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Any time after installing the [Dawnguard add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), you may hear a rumor from an innkeeper or [guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") about someone new in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"): *"People say there's someone in Riften that can... change your face. Make you look completely different. Do you believe that?"* Your quest journal will update with the objective to locate the face sculptor. Your map will not be updated with a quest marker, but if you travel to Riften, a guard will make a negative comment about the face sculptor, conveniently providing her location: *"Take my advice, don't listen to that talk of the "face sculptor" down in the [Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"). "Face butcher" is more like it from what I've heard."* Make your way to the Ragged Flagon, located within Riften's sewer network and accessible through the [Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway"). Sitting alone on a bench is [Galathil](/wiki/Skyrim:Galathil "Skyrim:Galathil"), the face sculptor you're seeking.

Upon approaching her, she'll speak to you before you can say a word: *"Hmm, I suppose I can work with your face. After all, the sculptor cannot always choose the finest clay."* If you are a vampire, however, she will be able to tell and instead say, *"What have you done to yourself? I can't work with you in this state, night-walker."* You can ask her what she's talking about, or tell her you've already heard of her. Either way, she will subtly insult you, by implying that your appearance is not "artful" or referring to you as the "scum of Skyrim". She will then check to see if you are a client, asking *"So are you here as a client? Shall I remake your face?"* unless you are a vampire, in which case she'll tell you *"But, my techniques only work on the living, not those that have crossed over into undeath."*

At this point, you can choose to have your appearance changed, back out, or question her qualifications. If you tell her you'll have to think about it, she'll respond, *"Indeed. It is no small thing to submit yourself to the flesh sculptor's knife."* and begin to read a book. You are still able to approach her again with the same options if you do this. If you question her, she'll answer defensively, telling you how experienced she is: *"I have not always been a ragged beggar. I learned my art from the masters of the art of flesh sculpture. I studied with the Faculty of Chirurgeons in Cloudrest. I walked with the Hollow-Faced Men of Nohotogrha for three years. I count the nobility of both the Empire and the Dominion among my clients"*, and then angrily add *"And yet, I have fallen so low that I must justify myself to a wanderer in the sewers of this backwater of the world."*

If you decide you would like her to change your appearance, it costs 1000 gold. If you can afford it, she'll say, *"Hmm. Very well. Just tell me what you desire - beauty or hideous deformity, nothing is beyond my skill"*, but if you don't have enough gold, she'll be offended and dismiss you: *"Despite my present low estate, I am no beggar. Begone until you have the coin to warrant my skills."*

When you pay her the gold, you will enter a screen nearly identical to the initial [character creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Character_Creation "Skyrim:Character Creation") option from beginning your game. You can change almost all aspects of your appearance, the only exceptions being your character's race or sex. There is no limit to the amount of times you can repeat this quest.

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked when you complete this quest:

-  **A New You**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") (20 points/Bronze) — Change your face

## Notes

- Despite taking place in Riften, this quest does not count towards [Thane of the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Rift "Skyrim:Thane of the Rift").
- Vampires cannot get their faces changed. You must [cure your vampirism](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism#Curing_Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism") in order to start this quest.
- Changing, or even overhauling, your appearance will not impair any NPC's ability to recognize you. Therefore, it cannot be used to, for example, erase bounties or start relations over with an NPC you've fallen out of favor with by making them think you're a different person.

## Bugs

- Occasionally, pushing "Done" in the character customization screen will have no effect. The only way to leave the screen in this instance is to load a previous save. It is unclear whether the face sculptor can ever be used on a save that exhibits this bug, but it is possible for other saves to use the sculptor. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Surgery (DLC1Surgery) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Locate the face sculptor in Riften |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Talk to the face sculptor in the Ragged Flagon |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 50.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1Surgery stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1Surgery`.

# Skyrim:Sven and Hilde's House

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Sven and Hilde's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sven+and+Hilde%27s+House)) | | |

| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Sven and Hilde's House

**Sven and Hilde's House** is a small residence at the western end of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), located next to the [Riverwood Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood_Trader "Skyrim:Riverwood Trader").

It is the home of [Hilde](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilde "Skyrim:Hilde") and her son [Sven](/wiki/Skyrim:Sven "Skyrim:Sven"), the local bard. It consists of one zone, *[Sven and Hilde's House](#Sven_and_Hilde.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Hilde](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilde "Skyrim:Hilde")  [Sven](/wiki/Skyrim:Sven "Skyrim:Sven") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") \* |

\* Becomes a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") only if the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Lovely_Letter "Skyrim:A Lovely Letter") is completed in his favor

## Related Quests

- **[A Lovely Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Lovely_Letter "Skyrim:A Lovely Letter")**: Use a forged letter to resolve a love triangle.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Sven and Hilde's House

Sven and Hilde's House, interior

It is a one-room house with no dividing lines between the areas. Straight ahead is the fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") and a kettle containing two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") at its base, and a respawning meat barrel to the right. To the left of the door is a chair, a few barrels, and a non-respawning cupboard in the corner with a respawning food barrel nearby. To the left of the fireplace is a table with a bucket containing two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), one bottle each of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and two leveled one-handed weapons—a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") and a [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"). Both weapons can be up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality at level 23. Hanging above the table are harvestable [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and [raw food](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Food "Skyrim:Raw Food"). There is one dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), two portions of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), and three [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant").

To the right of the door is a non-respawning dresser with a bottle of [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"), two samples each of elves ear and frost mirriam, and four garlic bulbs sitting on it, along with a respawning food barrel beside it. Hanging above the dresser is another set of harvestable ingredients—one dried frost mirriam, one dried elves ear, and three garlic braids. There is a small table with two chairs in the middle of the house by the fireplace, which serves as the dining table; it is set with one bottle each of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and alto wine, as well as one loaf and one piece of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). The shelves to the right of the fire contain some general household items, and four bottles each of wine and alto wine. There are two owned beds by the far right wall. The bed with a chest (non-respawning) at one end is Sven's and the one without a chest is Hilde's. Between the beds is a non-respawning end table holding one bottle of Nord mead.

## Notes

- The front door has a novice-level lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Sven%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Sven's House") to which is carried by both Hilde and Sven.
- After completing the quest [A Lovely Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Lovely_Letter "Skyrim:A Lovely Letter") in Sven's favor, all low-value items become free to take, and both beds become usable.
- There is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning") to the right of the front door, as well as two respawning food barrels a short distance to the left. Another two respawning food barrels can be found behind the house, in the east corner.

# Skyrim:Swift as an Arrow

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Learn how to craft and use [Telekinesis Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis_Arrow "Skyrim:Telekinesis Arrow").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Automatically added after purchasing the [Arcane Archer Pack](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Archer_Pack "Skyrim:Arcane Archer Pack") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") |
| Location(s): | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") |
| Reward: | [*Spell Tome: Telekinesis Arrows*](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Telekinesis_Arrows "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Telekinesis Arrows"), ability to craft [Telekinesis Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis_Arrow "Skyrim:Telekinesis Arrow") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE002\_TelekinesisArrowQuest |
| Added by: | [Arcane Archer Pack](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Archer_Pack "Skyrim:Arcane Archer Pack") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons") | | |

Learn the art of telekinesis archery

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Gain entrance to the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").
2. Read the [research notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis_Arrows_Research_Notes "Skyrim:Telekinesis Arrows Research Notes") and take the [spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Telekinesis_Arrows "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Telekinesis Arrows") from [the Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum").

## Detailed Walkthrough

**Note: This quest was originally added to your journal upon installing the [Arcane Archer Pack](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Archer_Pack "Skyrim:Arcane Archer Pack") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). With the release of the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition"), this quest no longer appears in your journal. The [Spell Tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Telekinesis_Arrows "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Telekinesis Arrows") and [Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis_Arrows_Research_Notes "Skyrim:Telekinesis Arrows Research Notes") added by the Creation can still be acquired from [the Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum") in the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), and [Telekinesis Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis_Arrow "Skyrim:Telekinesis Arrow") can still be crafted.**

Once you've installed the Arcane Archer Pack Creation, you will receive this quest directing you to the College of Winterhold to learn more about a spell tome which has been uncovered. The tome in question, [*Spell Tome: Telekinesis Arrows*](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Telekinesis_Arrows "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Telekinesis Arrows"), is held in the Arcanaeum, requiring you to first gain access to the college in order to proceed. See the [First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons") quest walkthrough for more information on how to join the college.

Locate the spell tome on the counter in front of [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub"). Simply picking it up will advance the quest. However, you must read the tome in order to learn the related [Telekinesis Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis_Arrows "Skyrim:Telekinesis Arrows") lesser power, which must be used to control the arrows. Reading the nearby [*Telekinesis Arrows Research Notes*](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis_Arrows_Research_Notes "Skyrim:Telekinesis Arrows Research Notes") will teach you how to craft [Telekinesis Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis_Arrow "Skyrim:Telekinesis Arrow"), provides an introductory description of how the arrows function and completes the quest.

## Quest Stages

| Swift as an Arrow (ccBGSSSE002\_TelekinesisArrowQuest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 0 |  | I've been told a lost Spell Tome has been found, which allows one to craft special arrows that can be controlled with a Lesser Telekinesis Power. I should head to the College of Winterhold to learn more. *Objective 0:* Find the Telekinesis Arrow Tome |
| 10 |  | I've found the Tome, and learned the Lesser Telekinesis Power, but I need to read the research notes to understand how to craft and use the arrows. *Objective 10:* Read the Research Note |
| 20 | ☑ | I've found the Telekinesis Arrows tome, and have learned how to craft and use them from the research notes. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE002_TelekinesisArrowQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE002_TelekinesisArrowQuest`.
