Swindler's Den

**Swindler's Den** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains only one zone, *[Swindler's Den](#Swindler.27s_Den)*.

## Related Quests

- **[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")**: Find a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") who is on the run from [her past](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth").

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo").
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout.
- **[Rare Gifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts")**: Do a favor by finding a rare item.
- **[Retrieval](/wiki/Skyrim:Retrieval "Skyrim:Retrieval")**: Journey to a random location to retrieve a fragment of [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad").
- **[Salty Sea-Dogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Salty_Sea-Dogs "Skyrim:Salty Sea-Dogs")**: Find some [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine-Cut_Void_Salts "Skyrim:Fine-Cut Void Salts") for an inexperienced [sea captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

A banner flies from a post to the right of the entrance, with a barrel with a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top and a bandit to the left. An [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), an [Imperial light helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Light Helmet"), a [hide helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Helmet "Skyrim:Hide Helmet"), and a [steel helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Helmet") are on short posts around the main post. Behind the entrance is a bedroll next to a barrel with a lit lantern and a piece of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") on top and a set of [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") directly beneath.

### Swindler's Den

Upon entering there is a narrow passage descending into a large chamber where two bandits are discussing current events. There is a table with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") on top. Beside this is a flat-topped rock with a crate, a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sack, and three loose [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). Behind this is a patch of [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungi, with a second sample in a bucket beside it. There is also an unowned bedroll with another bottle of Nord mead laid out on the ground, and above it all is a ledge which can be used as a shortcut back to the exit later. To the west are a practice dummy and a wooden block by a rock pillar, with a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat") on top, a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and an open crate containing a sprig of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") and a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") beside it. At the rear of the chamber, on a ledge illuminated by a hole in the roof, is an unlocked chest.

A passage out of this room is also in the rear of the chamber on the north wall. Partway along the passage is an illuminated alcove on the left, containing a random [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") and quiver of [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"). The passage then emerges onto a ledge overlooking a second chamber with a campfire and two bandits attending. There is a whole skeever spitted over the fire, which you can harvest for a [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"), and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") hanging below. There are two unowned bedrolls around the fire and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") leaning against a pile of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood"), with two loose pieces nearby. To the left is a bucket containing a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), a potato, and [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). In the western corner of the chamber is a crate with a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel") and a random minor potion on top, while against the south wall is another crate with an iron helmet and a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets") on top.

There is a passage leading from this chamber on the east wall. The passage takes a couple of turns as it rises before entering a large chamber containing three bandits on the main level mostly sitting at a row of long wooden tables, with a fourth bandit, a magic-user, standing on a ledge at the rear overlooking the chamber. On the tables are four bottles of Nord mead, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), and a [venison chop](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison_Chop "Skyrim:Venison Chop"). Between two of the tables are a crate and two food sacks. Under the ledge to the east is a small square table with a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [silver necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Necklace"), an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"), and seventeen loose pieces of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on top. The table may be disrupted during the melee, so the loot may end up scattered on the ground. Upon entering the chamber and engaging the bandits, at least two additional bandits may converge from the adjoining chamber via the passage on the north wall. The magic user will engage you with ranged spells from the ledge. On the ground to the left of the next passage is a [deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide") by more firewood.

The passage passes an alcove on the right containing a straw bale with a skeleton partially buried in it and a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") on top, before turning to the east and climbing to the next chamber, where two more bandits can be found if they haven't already been dealt with. There is a small slightly raised section opposite where you enter containing several barrels, an unlocked chest, and a table with a deer hide on top. By the raised section are an extinguished campfire with four whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") hanging over it and a fifth on a wooden block beside the fire, and two bedrolls nearby. At the rear of the chamber is a second campfire with two more bedrolls beside it. On one of these is a copy of the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(book) "Skyrim:Thief (book)")*, and to the southeast are several barrels and crates beside another long table with four [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a cast iron pot containing two [raw rabbit legs](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg") and a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), and a potato. By the table are a food sack and a kettle containing two cabbages and a potato, while hanging above from two racks are two pheasants and three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). Just to the left of the exit on the south wall, on top of a rock formation are two [refined malachite](/wiki/Skyrim:Refined_Malachite "Skyrim:Refined Malachite") ingots and a [gold ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ingot "Skyrim:Gold Ingot") in an open crate and three food sacks.

The passage continues south, before turning west and leading out onto the ledge where the magic user was standing in the previous chamber. Along the front edge of the ledge on a crate is another deer hide, and the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") skill book *[Night Falls on Sentinel](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Falls_on_Sentinel "Skyrim:Night Falls on Sentinel")* will spawn here if you have [Rustleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Rustleif "Skyrim:Rustleif")'s quest [Rare Gifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts") active. Farther along to the west is a wooden block with an iron dagger on top and behind this is patch of [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") fungus. Take care as there are two [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") by the mouth of the passage leading onwards. Proceed through the passage as it takes a couple of turns before entering a partially flooded section. On the south and northwest walls are [Nordic barnacle clusters](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle_Cluster "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle Cluster"), with two more clusters at the bottom of the wooden ramp. The water is initially chest-high, but becomes shallow as you approach the back of a waterfall. Passing through the waterfall leads to a wooden ramp.

At the top of the ramp during the quest [In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need") you will find [Kematu](/wiki/Skyrim:Kematu "Skyrim:Kematu") and up to six [Alik'r Warriors](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Warrior "Skyrim:Alik'r Warrior"), each clothed in [Hammerfell garb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hammerfell_Garb "Skyrim:Hammerfell Garb"), [Redguard boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Boots "Skyrim:Redguard Boots") and [Alik'r hoods](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Hood "Skyrim:Alik'r Hood") and armed with a [scimitar](/wiki/Skyrim:Scimitar "Skyrim:Scimitar"), except for Kematu who has no Alik'r hood and is armed with two scimitars. On the right, at the top of the ramp, between several barrels is an unlocked boss chest. On the barrels are four bottles of Nord mead and a leveled potion of stamina. To the left is a patch of [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") fungus, with a second patch growing against the south wall. To the right of the chest, against the north wall are several crates with a whole salmon and a cast iron pot containing two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") on top. In front of this is an unowned bedroll. A passage heads north, passing an alcove lit by a brazier with an earthen ramp leading up. Find an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") in the wall at the base of the ramp. Ascending the earthen ramp will lead to the ledge in the first chamber, thus completing the circuit of Swindler's Den. On your left is a crate with a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") leaning against it and a quiver and two loose [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") on top. Jump down from the ledge to make your exit.

## Notes

- It is possible to climb up to the eastern ledge in the first chamber, which will allow you to backtrack through the cave and reach the boss and his chest without fighting most of the cave's inhabitants.
- It is possible to incite the bandits to fight the Alik'r, making the quest much easier. As an example, standing in the entrance to the large room and shooting an arrow up toward the entrance to the Alik'r area (with the bear traps in front of it) can draw the four bandits into a fight with the warriors. The ensuing fight can kill or wound most of the enemies, including Kematu.
- South of Swindler's Den is an unmarked [shrine of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Shrine of Stendarr"). On the altar is a [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), a [flawless amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Amethyst "Skyrim:Flawless Amethyst"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Twin Secrets](/wiki/Skyrim:Twin_Secrets "Skyrim:Twin Secrets")*, and a strongbox which may contain up to two random leveled [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems"), two random leveled pieces of [jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Jewelry "Skyrim:Jewelry"), and/or some gold.
- Southwest of Swindler's Den is an unmarked ruin containing a satchel, two [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), a [shrine to Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Shrine of Zenithar"), an [amulet of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Amulet of Zenithar"), and a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Second Seed, v5](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Second_Seed,_v5 "Skyrim:2920, Second Seed, v5")*.

## Bugs

- The normal bandit boss here is not tagged as a boss, preventing the location from being marked as cleared.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- If you side with Kematu during the quest In My Time Of Need, he will still appear at the back of the cave even after he has supposedly left for Hammerfell.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Sylgja's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Sylgja's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sylgja%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| ShorsStoneSylgjasHouse | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") along the main road. | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 2 |

Sylgja's House

**Sylgja's House** is a house in the small mining settlement of  [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"). It is located behind the outdoor campfire where the townsfolk gather every night.

It is the home of local miner [Sylgja](/wiki/Skyrim:Sylgja "Skyrim:Sylgja") who lives there alone. It consists of one area only, *[Sylgja's House](#Sylgja.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Sylgja](/wiki/Skyrim:Sylgja "Skyrim:Sylgja") |

## Sylgja's House

Inside Sylgja's House

As is common with houses in smaller settlements, the fireplace and the [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") are located opposite to the front door. There are three gold coins sitting on the mantelpiece. The southern part of the house holds little of interest – only two barrels, one of them with a huge [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") on top. Next to the fireplace is a dinner table with some food scattered around, two [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), a clove of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), three slices of [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and a head of [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). Adjacent to the table stands a cupboard with clutter, with a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") and a sample of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat") on top.

The northern corner of the house holds a set of shelves with two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and one of regular [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), as well as a few common books. A chest in the corner holds a sparse amount of items and the dresser underneath holds [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing"). Following the wall is an end table that holds clutter and has a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") on top and a food barrel. The corner also contains Sylgja's huge dinner table, which is set up for four although Sylgja always eats alone. It holds three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), two bottles of alto wine and one regular.

The double bed stands in the eastern alcove which also has a huge wardrobe with clothes, with a [sabre cat pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Pelt "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Pelt") on top. There is also a small table with two bottles of [nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and a chest with valuables at the foot of the bed. Two end tables hold clutter; one has four gold coins sitting on top, while the other has a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat "Skyrim:Hat") and a [potion of haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling") on top. On the floor, Sylgja has a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes "Skyrim:Shoes") and a hidden coin purse.

## Notes

- The chest at the foot of Sylgja's bed is *not* safe for storage.

# Skyrim:Tag, you're it!

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Secunda](/wiki/User:Secunda "User:Secunda"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Play a round of Tag with the children of a city.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Radiant |
| Location(s): | Radiant |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | WIGamesTag |

Playing tag in Solitude

## Quick Walkthrough

1. You are it!
2. Tag!
3. Bob and weave.

## Detailed Walkthrough

**Tag, you're it!** is a [game](/wiki/Skyrim:Activities#Interactions "Skyrim:Activities") that can be played with the children in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") and [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). With [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") installed, the game can be started with your [adopted children](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption") as well.

To play, initiate the game by offering or accepting the game from eligible children. The aim of the game is to avoid being tagged by whoever is "it". If you are it, you must try to tag someone else. The quest will update whenever "it" changes hands and quest arrows show who you can tag or who to avoid.

The game ends after 90 seconds of play and the quest is removed. This has no material benefit and is mostly just for fun.

## Notes

- Entering a new area while playing the game will usually cause the game to end and you may have to speak to the children again to play.
- Games are only playable from 8am until 9pm.
  - Adopted children can play tag at night if asked to.
- Starting a game of tag via your adopted child can cause all children in the area to play, even those who won't normally play.

## Bugs

- While [Fjotra](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") is following you during the quest [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella") initiating a game of tag can cause her to play the game allowing you and other players to tag her. However, because she is following you, she won't run after or tag anyone when she becomes it.
- If you fast travel during this quest, the children may end up fast traveling with you. **?**
- Starting a game with more than 4 children present will get all children running, but only 4 of them can be tagged. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Tag, you're it! (WIGamesTag) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
|  |  | *(Assigned as appropriate during the game)* *Objective 10:* <Alias=PlayerIsIt> is it. Keep away from <Alias=PlayerIsIt.PronounObj>  *Objective 20:* You're it! Tag someone. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage WIGamesTag stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest WIGamesTag`.

# Skyrim:Take the Hidden Treasure

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Krusty](/wiki/User:Krusty "User:Krusty"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Krusty](/wiki/User:Krusty "User:Krusty"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Torture the Brotherhood's prisoners for treasure.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Torture Victims](/wiki/Skyrim:Torture_Victim "Skyrim:Torture Victim") |
| Location(s): | [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary") |
| Reward: | 4x 1000-2000 gold (random) |
| ID: | DBTortureTreasureMiscObjective1 DBTortureTreasureMiscObjective2 DBTortureTreasureMiscObjective3 DBTortureTreasureMiscObjective4 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...](/wiki/Skyrim:Where_You_Hang_Your_Enemy%27s_Head... "Skyrim:Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...](/wiki/Skyrim:Where_You_Hang_Your_Enemy%27s_Head... "Skyrim:Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...") | | |

A good investment

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Purchase the torture room upgrade from [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory").
2. Talk repeatedly to any of the four torture victims in the [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary").
3. Find the hidden treasure and claim it for yourself.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After purchasing the torture room upgrade for the [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary") from [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory"), you will find four very [unlucky prisoners](/wiki/Skyrim:Torture_Victim "Skyrim:Torture Victim") who all have quite a bit of gold hidden away in the wilderness for one reason or another. Talk to any of the four abductees repeatedly and they will reveal the location of their hidden treasure. Your [journal](#Quest_Stages) will be updated with a new quest which points to the treasure's location. Now all you have to do is find the hidden treasure and claim it for yourself. You can interrogate all four victims at the same time to prevent multiple trips back to the sanctuary. You may only claim the treasure once, as it does not respawn.

### The Inheritance

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Old woman | *"Why are you people doing this?"*  *"Is it information you want?"*  *"This... this is about the inheritance, isn't it? All right! I'll tell you where I've hidden it."*  *"It's in a hollowed-out tree stump. In the marsh, south of Solitude. Now please, you'll let me go now. Right?"*   *"Why don't you be a dear and let me go now. All right? I won't say a word to anyone. Our little secret. I promise."* | The tree stump south of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") |

Even after the elderly [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") practically hands you her inheritance in exchange for freedom, you can do nothing but let her hang in the torture room and claim the gold. Traveling to the [Abandoned Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Shack "Skyrim:Abandoned Shack") is a quicker option than [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), and you are bound to have it on your map. From the shack, proceed through the marshes in a southwesterly direction until you reach a small island several yards northeast of the [Apprentice Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Apprentice_Stone "Skyrim:The Apprentice Stone"). It is now a simple matter of taking the gold from the hollowed-out tree stump.

### No More Pain

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Red-haired man | *"I'll tell you anything. Anything! Just please stop... hurting me..."*  *"I just...can't take the pain. Not a second longer."*  *"I'll give you money. Treasure. I have some things hidden away. Take them all. They're yours. Just please... stop."*  *"Just north of Windhelm. There's a hollowed-out rock. I have some things hidden in there. Take them! They're yours."*   *"I've told you everything I can. I don't know what else you could want..."* | The rock near [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |

The hollowed-out rock sits out in the open, near the walls of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), on the northeastern side. The easiest path is traveling to [Hollyfrost Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hollyfrost_Farm "Skyrim:Hollyfrost Farm") and crossing the river. If you are in Windhelm, you will have to swim in an easterly direction from the city gate to get around the walls and reach the rock. In any case, locate the anonymous-looking rock halfway up the mountain, and beware of the [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") or other dangers in the area.

### Kill me and be done with it...

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Long-haired man | *"Please..."*  *"What is it you want?"*  *"Just... just stop. And I'll tell you where I've hidden my treasure."*  *"It's... in a hollowed-out rock. In the tundra. A bit west of Whiterun. Now please... please stop."*   *"Oh gods, you've taken everything I have. Just kill me and be done with it..."* | The rock near [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") |

This rock will spawn due west of [Pelagia Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagia_Farm "Skyrim:Pelagia Farm"), south of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). Travel to the farm and head west towards the mountainside. There is no need to climb the mountain; just stay on the ground and you will reach the rock in no time. It is squeezed in between two larger rocks.

### Canceled Wedding

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Young woman | *"You... you can't do this to me."*  *"Do you have any idea who I am? When my father hears about this, he will gut you."*  *"Ah, now I understand. This is about my father's hidden cache, isn't it? The dowry for my wedding?"*  *"Ha! Well it's safely hidden away, in a hollowed-out tree stump. Just outside Riften, tucked away nice and secure. You'll never find it."*   *"Damn it. I gave it away, didn't I?"* | The tree stump near [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") |

This victim's father apparently saved up money for his daughter's upcoming wedding and stashed it in a secure place outside Riften. With her being tied up inside the Sanctuary, the wedding is obviously canceled, so the savings are yours to take. Travel to [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") and proceed northwest, a few feet past [Merryfair Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Merryfair_Farm "Skyrim:Merryfair Farm"). The hollowed-out tree stump is easy to spot and the gold is yours to keep.

## Notes

- The hollowed-out rocks and tree stumps don't exist until you have interrogated the victims.
- The rewards will, in most cases, easily cover your expenses for the torture room, and even net a maximum profit of 3000 gold. If your luck does not hold, you may actually lose up to 1000 gold. It is advised to save before talking to your victim and traveling to the location to check.
- As the torture victims are completely restrained, they can easily be used to train skills on, as long as they are healed.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DBTortureTreasureMiscObjective1 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DBTortureTreasureMiscObjective1`.

# Skyrim:Take Up Arms

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. | [SR-qico-Companions.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Companions.png) | **Prove you are worthy to join the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Various |
| Location(s): | [Pelagia Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagia_Farm "Skyrim:Pelagia Farm"), [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") |
| Reward: | Membership in the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") |
| ID: | C00 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** One [Radiant Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions#Radiant_Quests "Skyrim:Companions"), [Proving Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proving_Honor "Skyrim:Proving Honor") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | One [Radiant Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions#Radiant_Quests "Skyrim:Companions"), [Proving Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proving_Honor "Skyrim:Proving Honor") | | |

Your first encounter with the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Locate the headquarters of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").
2. Find and talk to [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane").
3. Prove yourself worthy against [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas").
4. Make yourself useful to the higher-ranked members.

### Find the Companions

On your way to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), you may come across members of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions"), specifically [Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress"), [Ria](/wiki/Skyrim:Ria "Skyrim:Ria"), and [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas"), battling a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") among the sparse crops outside [Pelagia Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagia_Farm "Skyrim:Pelagia Farm"). If you want to participate in this fight, make sure to head straight to the farm once you arrive in the vicinity of Whiterun. If you delay for even a short time, the Companions will have already defeated the giant before you can join the fray, resulting in Aela taunting you for your lack of assistance. If you delay for too long, you may miss the Companions entirely, as they will slowly walk to the main gates of Whiterun and enter the city after the battle. Note that neither of these results has any negative consequences in your dealings with the Companions. If you are present when the giant dies, Aela will actively seek you out and will, depending on the outcome of the battle, either commend or taunt your battle skills. In both cases, however, she will tell you about the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") and point you towards [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane") in [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr").

This quest can also be started by speaking with select [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") citizens or Jorrvaskr residents, who will suggest you go speak with Kodlak.

### Jorrvaskr

Jorrvaskr is a legendary mead hall and the oldest building in Whiterun; it is located in the Wind District, up the eastern set of stairs from the Gildergreen. Inside the building, you will witness a friendly brawl between newcomers [Athis](/wiki/Skyrim:Athis "Skyrim:Athis") and [Njada Stonearm](/wiki/Skyrim:Njada_Stonearm "Skyrim:Njada Stonearm") while the other members cheer. The harbinger of the Companions, [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane"), will most likely be in the northern room of the Living Quarters, busy talking to [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") about what seem to be important matters. When asked about membership, Kodlak will consider you worthy, while Vilkas will disagree. After a brief argument between the two, Kodlak will ask about your battle skills. Regardless of your answer, Kodlak will order Vilkas to escort you to the yard for a quick sparring session. Follow Vilkas to the yard and pick up the fight. Make sure not to use magic, a bound weapon, or an enchanted weapon, for if you do Vilkas will temporarily stop the session. If you only have enchanted weapons, unequip them and use your fists. Take a few swings at Vilkas and prove your worth. Once Vilkas asks you to stop, accept your status as a 'whelp' and the fact that you will run errands for now.

### A Few Errands

Vilkas will hand you his [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas%27s_Sword "Skyrim:Vilkas's Sword") for sharpening. Take it to the best smith in town, [Eorlund Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane"), who works at the [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge") just up the stairs from the Jorrvaskr entrance. Eorlund will briefly explain how newcomers tend to get bossed around upon joining the Companions, and will then ask for a favor. He will give you a [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Aela's Shield") for [Aela](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress"), who can be found talking to [Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor") in the living quarters. Similar to the conversation between Kodlak and Vilkas, it becomes apparent that the Companions hide a few secrets, although none of them will share them with you at this time. When you hand Aela the shield, she will thank you for the favor and summon [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") to escort you to your new quarters, where a free bed will be available. Farkas will introduce you to a few of the other newcomers and will also offer you a job, which will be one of his radiant quests. You can choose to ignore his request, as seven different [radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions#Radiant_Quests "Skyrim:Companions") will now be available from the guild members, and you must complete at least one of them before your next major assignment, [Proving Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proving_Honor "Skyrim:Proving Honor").

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked when you complete this quest:

-  **Take Up Arms** (10 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- In the living quarters, Aela and Farkas' dialogue will differ. If you met them earlier near Pelagia Farm, they will both recognize you; if you went straight to Jorrvaskr, they will just greet you like a newcomer.
- If you manage to drop Vilkas' health to zero during the test, he'll qualify your performance as "most impressive" rather than just "not bad".
- Athis and Njada Stonearm's brawl can potentially go on forever if you first enter Jorrvaskr at a high level. Going into the basement will end the fight.

## Bugs

- If you place [Vilkas's sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas%27s_Sword "Skyrim:Vilkas's Sword") on a weapon rack or plaque, the quest can still be completed by talking to Eorlund, and the sword will disappear from the rack/plaque. However, the slot the sword occupied can never be used again.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- When training with Vilkas, he may spew combat taunts at you.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, addresses this issue. The taunts were never supposed to happen, so he is now being temporarily made a player teammate during the sparring match so that the taunts will be suppressed.
- If Aela's Shield is pickpocketed off of her after you've given it to her, it will end up getting stacked with other common Steel Shields, causing the entire stack to in essence become her shield.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.4, fixes this bug.

  - CompanionsMiscObjective: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage C00 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest C00`.

# Skyrim:Taking Care of Business

Use coercion to collect Haelga's debt

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") in the [Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon").
2. Collect the debts:
   - [Keerava](/wiki/Skyrim:Keerava "Skyrim:Keerava")
   - [Bersi Honey-Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Bersi_Honey-Hand "Skyrim:Bersi Honey-Hand")
   - [Haelga](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga "Skyrim:Haelga")
3. Return to Brynjolf.

### There's More Where That Came From

[Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") tells you to meet him in the [Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") underneath [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") if you're interested in more lucrative operations like [the one he arranged earlier](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Chance_Arrangement "Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement"). The only way to reach the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") headquarters at this point is through the [Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway"). The entrance is through an inconspicuous gate on the lower level of Riften. You'll have to fight or avoid several enemies; more detail on what you'll encounter is below.

Ratway walkthrough →

Down some stairs and at the end of the corridor are [Drahff](/wiki/Skyrim:Drahff "Skyrim:Drahff") and [Hewnon Black-Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Hewnon_Black-Skeever "Skyrim:Hewnon Black-Skeever"), two lowlifes who will be discussing some kind of plot to undermine the Guild. They will both attack on sight. If you wish to sneak past them, keep in mind that when their conversation ends, Hewnon will crouch by the fire with his back to you, and Drahff will begin patrolling the corridor between Hewnon and the entrance.

Take a right into a room with a bedroll, and then another right to a two-level room with a raised drawbridge directly across from you. The "correct" way to go about this would be to jump down to the lower level, but if you know Whirlwind Sprint, you can use it to skip the dungeon. Use the shout to get across the gap to the right of the drawbridge, where there is a small space of ledge under the railing that you can land on. You can then just jump onto and over the railing where you'll be in the last room of the dungeon. If you went to the lower level, there's also a gate to the left which can be a shortcut to the final room if you are proficient in [picking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") expert-level locks; if not, you'll have to take the long way around. The "scenic" route is full of traps, but there's a unique item as well.

Southwest of the expert-locked gate is a short corridor ending in a brazier and a door. Opening it without disabling the [tension cable](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") on the bottom right side will make two [spears](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") shoot out from the wall to the left. Beyond is a room with an oil slick on the floor and a lantern above. The south door leads onward to a room with five bear traps scattered near the entrance. [Gian the Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Gian_the_Fist "Skyrim:Gian the Fist"), who has the [Gloves of the Pugilist](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloves_of_the_Pugilist "Skyrim:Gloves of the Pugilist"), is across the room and will attack on sight. Beware, as his detection level is very high; he will probably sense you and attack even if you have a high [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") skill. The gloves may be useful later during this quest if you choose to brawl anyone. There's also an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") in the alcove to the left.

In the next room, go up the stairs, watching out for the pressure plate and corresponding battering ram that will hit you in the back if you're not careful. After this, a gate opens up to circular room overgrown with plants. In the center is a wood chopping block with an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe") stuck in it. Turn north again and you'll be in the last room which contains a hostile [lowlife](/wiki/Skyrim:Lowlife "Skyrim:Lowlife") and a [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). Be sure to drop the drawbridge via the lever for future ease of access, and pick up the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") skill book *[Beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_(book) "Skyrim:Beggar (book)")* from the table. The door to the Ragged Flagon is to the east.

The Thieves Guild headquarters is rather run-down, and as you circle around the shallow pool to the bar proper, you'll overhear a conversation about the sorry state of affairs:

*"I wasn't certain I'd ever see you again!"*

**[Vekel the Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Vekel_the_Man "Skyrim:Vekel the Man")**: *Give it up, Brynjolf... those days are over.*
**Brynjolf**: *I'm telling you, this one is different...*
**[Dirge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dirge "Skyrim:Dirge")**: *We've all heard that one before, Bryn! Quit kidding yourself.*
**Vekel**: *It's time to face the truth, old friend. You, Vex, Mercer... you're all part of a dying breed. Things are changing!*
**Brynjolf**: *Dying breed, eh? Well what do you call that then!*

At this point Brynjolf will turn around and, if you are close enough, approach to say, *"Well, well... Color me impressed lad/lass. I wasn't certain I'd ever see you again!"*

And you'll have three options. If you say that you got through the Ratway easily, he will be doubly impressed, saying, *"Reliable and headstrong? You're turning out to be quite the prize!"* If you claim you nearly died or point out the less-than-lovely state of the Guild, he will be annoyed, saying, *"No risk, no reward. That's the way it goes, so you better get used to it."* or *"If you were expecting a palace, then maybe you're not cut out for this line of work. Our methods involve secrecy and discretion."*, respectively. In any case, he will then go on to ask if you're up to *"handling a few deadbeats"* for him. *"They owe our organization some serious coin and they've decided not to pay. I want you to explain to them the error of their ways,"* Brynjolf will explain, then tell you who they are at your inquiry: *"Keerava, Bersi Honey-Hand and Haelga. Do this right, and I can promise you a permanent place in our organization."*

After Brynjolf tells you to get going, the quest will update with the three debts to recover. You can head topside immediately (you'll have to go back through the Ratway), but it also pays to stay a bit longer and ask Brynjolf about the marks. His dialogue will reveal weaknesses to exploit for each: [Keerava](/wiki/Skyrim:Keerava "Skyrim:Keerava") has a soft spot for family, [Bersi](/wiki/Skyrim:Bersi_Honey-Hand "Skyrim:Bersi Honey-Hand") has a priceless - and fragile - urn, and [Haelga](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga "Skyrim:Haelga") has her devotion to [Dibella](/wiki/Lore:Dibella "Lore:Dibella"), goddess of beauty.

The debts may be collected in any order you choose, but keep in mind that after you have two debtors in line, the last - whomever that may be - will cave immediately, having heard how you dealt with the others.

### Keerava's Debt

Keerava runs [Riften's](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") only inn, [the Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb"), next to the market. Once inside, you'll find her behind the bar, tending to her patrons. Tell her you have a message from Brynjolf and she will say *"I'll already told that buffoon I'm not paying you people a single coin!"* When you say it wasn't a request, she'll be stubborn. *"Look around you, I'm barely keeping this rathole together. The war's seen to that."* You'll have two options now. You can either brawl with her to collect the debt, or you can try the route that Brynjolf suggested if you talked to him.

Find [Talen-Jei](/wiki/Skyrim:Talen-Jei "Skyrim:Talen-Jei"), another [Argonian](/wiki/Lore:Argonian "Lore:Argonian") in the tavern, who is Keerava's lover. He will be suspicious of you, but if you tell him to talk some sense into her, he will say, *"With the rumors going around about how poorly your Guild's been doing, she's become much too bold. I'm not that foolish. The last thing I want is a war with your people."* If you ask for his cooperation, you will have it. *"Look, I'm only telling you this because I care for her. Don't mistake this as acceptance for what you do. Keerava has some family at a farm just inside of Morrowind. If you mention you know about it, she might just listen to you. Just please, don't harm anyone. I couldn't bear the thought."* Return to Keerava and she will give up the money, petrified with fear.

If you return to Brynjolf after receiving Keerava's payment, but before finishing all three debtors, you can offer him Keerava's payment on its own, to which he will respond *"She was the toughest of the bunch. Honestly, I'm amazed she didn't kick you out of the Bee and Barb herself."*

If Keerava is the last debtor you collect from, she will instead say, *"Look, everything was all just a misunderstanding. I didn't mean to tell Brynjolf to go jump off the pier. You'll tell him I said sorry, yes? Take this. Every single coin I owe is there, I swear it."*

### Bersi's Debt

Bersi's priceless urn

Bersi Honey-Hand is the owner of the [Pawned Prawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawned_Prawn "Skyrim:Pawned Prawn") general store, to the west of the Bee and Barb. He's usually behind the counter, with his precious Dwemer Urn sitting on a cabinet right across from him. Tell him that you have a message, and he will be disgusted. *"Wha... what? Oh, it's one of you people. So, Brynjolf doesn't even bother to show up himself anymore, eh? What's this message?"* The two options presented lead to different dialogue: *"Petty threats and fist waving are not going to sway me. You people are all talk, and everyone knows it! Pay you to protect me? You can't even protect yourselves!"* if you threaten him and *"You're gouging me for what little coin I make and you can't even protect yourselves? Ridiculous!"* if you say he knows what it is. The end result is the same; either walk away, or brawl.

If you're not up to fisticuffs with him, though, you can always duke it out with the urn. It's across from Bersi, ready for the smashing. Take out your weapon or spell (it will take a few hits to break it, so you may not want to use a bow) and get to it. Bersi and his wife [Drifa](/wiki/Skyrim:Drifa "Skyrim:Drifa") will yell out as you do, but once the urn is shattered beyond repair Bersi will say *"No! That urn was priceless!"* Ask him if he wants you to break anything else, and he will pay you: *"All right! I get it. I'll pay on time from now on. Just don't smash anything else. Here, take your gold and leave me in peace."*

If you return to Brynjolf after receiving Bersi's payment, but before finishing all three debtors, you can offer him Bersi's payment on its own, to which he will respond *"I wasn't sure that he'd see the light, but I'm sure you "explained" it to him. Well done!"*

If Bersi is the last one you visit, he will say *"Oh! There's no need for that. I know why you're here. Tell Brynjolf not to worry about it anymore. Oh! And look, I even have the payment I owed. Here, take it."*

### Haelga's Debt

Haelga runs the eponymous [Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga%27s_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Haelga's Bunkhouse"), north of the Bee and Barb. She is dismissive of you from the get-go, saying *"If you're looking for a room, try the Bee and Barb. This place is for the working man."* Tell her you have a message from Brynjolf and she will say *"What does he want now? I already explained to him that you can't get blood from a stone."* Now you can either brawl, or come at the problem from another angle.

Around the corner to the east is a set of drawers, upon which sits a golden statue of Dibella, Divine of beauty, to whom Haelga is devoted. Swipe it and go back to Haelga. Threaten to drop the statue down a well and she will crack: *"Not Lady Dibella? No, please! I can't lose her! I get the message. Here, take your gold. I hope you choke on it!"*

If you return to Brynjolf after receiving Haelga's payment, but before finishing all three debtors, you can offer him Haelga's payment on its own, to which he will respond *"She's as stubborn as she is beautiful, isn't she? Glad you found a way to get her to pay."*

If Haelga is last, she will be afraid: *"I know who you are. You've been terrorizing the entire city. Please, there's no need for that here. Message understood. Here, I even have the payment!"*

### Bring Home the Bacon

When you return to him (once again through the Ratway), Brynjolf will have different sets of dialogue depending on whether any of the three died, and whether you still have the gold you were sent to collect.

- If you don't have enough gold, and at least one is dead, whether killed by you or not: *"You have wax in your ears? I said no one dies. We're not assassins. Well guess what... now you've inherited their debt. Don't come back to me until you have every last coin."*

- If you don't have enough gold, but everyone is alive: *"So I've heard. Thanks to you, this should be the last time they forget to pay. One small detail though - I need all of the gold they gave you. No one skims around here. Come back when you've got every last coin."*

You will have to acquire the remainder yourself. Once you do have enough gold, you can proceed.

- If one or more are dead: *"Are you daft? I told you not kill any of them. How much clearer do you need me to be? How about the gold? Did you remember to bring it or is that too difficult an instruction as well."* Confirm it's all there and he will continue, still angry, *"I suppose it's not a total loss then. Let me give you a piece of advice. If you want to make some serious coin in this business you need to listen to rules. Now, on to other things."*

- If all are alive: *"So, job's done and you even brought the gold. Best of all you did it clean. I like that. Dumping bodies and keeping the guards quiet can be expensive."* Hand over the gold and he will say, *"Well done. And it would seem I owe you something in return. Here you go, I think you'll find these quite useful."* He will hand you a nice bonus of three [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"): one [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), one potion of fortify health, and one fortifying a random [stealth skill](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealth "Skyrim:Stealth").

Ask him what's next and he will continue: *"Despite your mistakes, I see more potential in you than half the snot-nosed footpads that stumble their way into the Flagon. I'm going to put my neck on the line. We need people like you in our outfit."* or *"Judging from how well you handled those shopkeepers, I'd say you've done more than simply prove yourself. We need people like you in our outfit."*

Regardless, when you show interest at more gold, he will say, *"That's the spirit! Larceny's in your blood... the telltale sign of a practiced thief. I think you'll do more than just fit in around here."* You can ask him about the rumors - that the Guild is in dire straits - and he will be dismissive: *"We've run into a rough patch lately, but it's nothing to be concerned about. Tell you what. You keep making us coin and I'll worry about everything else. Fair enough?"* Reply "fair enough" and he will get the show on the road. *"Now if there are no more questions, how about following me and I'll show you what we're all about."*

This will end Taking Care of Business and start the next quest, [Loud and Clear](/wiki/Skyrim:Loud_and_Clear "Skyrim:Loud and Clear").

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked at the end of this quest:

-  **Taking Care of Business** (10 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- As soon as this quest ends, the alternate entrance in Riften's graveyard will become available, providing a direct route to the [Cistern](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon_-_Cistern "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon - Cistern").
- When given the chance to brawl, if you choose the non-brawling dialogue option, the debtor will refuse to speak to you afterward. Your only options to complete the quest at that point will be to use Brynjolf's suggested method, or kill them.
- If broken, Bersi's urn will remain broken for the rest of the game, while Haelga's Statue of Dibella will eventually return to its original position.

## Bugs

- If Talen-Jei dies before the quest is started, it may not start at all.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.1, addresses this issue. Talen-Jei is made essential.
- If Drifa has died prior to ending **A Chance Arrangement**, this quest will not be able to start.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the console command `setstage TG02 10` to start the quest manually.
- Bersi's prize urn can appear unbreakable. **?**
  - Winning a brawl against him instead advances the quest, or you can also leave him as the last person, as he will comply without further intimidation.
- Sometimes this quest will complete and you will be unable to start the next one, even through console commands. This means that if you go into the Ragged Flagon Cistern, you will be trespassing and all of the thieves will turn hostile.
  -  This can be fixed by using the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `setstage TG02 10` and finishing it before entering the Cistern.
  -  If the step above doesn't work, it can be fixed by using the command `setstage TG02 0` before entering the Cistern.
- If you make your follower steal Haelga's Statue of Dibella, the optional quest will not be completed. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Taking Care of Business (TG01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Brynjolf has promised me more work if I'm able to locate him at a tavern called the Ragged Flagon. Judging from the dangerous nature of its location, it seems as though he's having me perform some type of initiation, but I can't be certain. *Objective 10:* Locate Brynjolf at the Ragged Flagon |
| 20 |  | After successfully locating the Ragged Flagon, Brynjolf has given me a new assignment. Three business owners in Riften are proving to be a thorn in his side and I'm supposed to teach them the error of their ways. I should speak to Brynjolf about these townspeople in the event that they prove to be as stubborn as I'm expecting them to be. *Objective 20:* Collect Keerava's debt  *Objective 30:* Collect Bersi Honey-Hand's debt  *Objective 40:* Collect Haelga's debt |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Return to Brynjolf |
| 200 | ☑ | I've dealt with the three troublesome business owners in Riften as Brynjolf had specified. Perhaps now that I've proven my worth to Brynjolf, I can discover more about this mysterious organization that he represents. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 21:* (Optional) Use Talen-Jei to get to Keerava  *Objective 31:* (Optional) Smash Bersi's prized Dwarven Urn  *Objective 41:* (Optional) Steal Haelga's Statue of Dibella |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 12, 30, 35, 40, 42, 45, 47.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TG01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TG01`.

# Skyrim:Talking Stone Camp

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Giant Camp.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Giant_Camp.png) | Giant Camp: Talking Stone Camp ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Talking+Stone+Camp)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 2 |
| Occupants | |
| [Giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant"), [Mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| TalkingStoneCampExterior01, TalkingStoneCampExterior02 | |
| Region | |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | |
| Location | |
| Northeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") South of [Orotheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Orotheim "Skyrim:Orotheim") | |

Talking Stone Camp

**Talking Stone Camp** is a [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") northeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead").

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Giant "Skyrim:Bounty: Giant")**: Kill a problematic [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") for a bounty reward. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Walkthrough

Two [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") and two [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") occupy the camp and the nearby area, with one giant in the camp and the other giant herding the mammoths to the northeast. A large campfire is in the middle of the camp, with two [charred skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") on fire-hardened stakes cooking over it. Typical of giant camps, many painted stones, [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes"), and mammoth ribs and skulls are found throughout the area. North of the campfire is an empty stone bowl with a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), a random [healing potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potions"), and a random [fortify skill potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Potion_of_Alteration "Skyrim:Potions") beside it. To the left is another stone bowl holding many [soul gem fragments](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem_Fragment "Skyrim:Soul Gem Fragment") and a random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). Nearby to the north is a tree stump with a [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") fungus and a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). To the left of the chest is a large painted stone with several giant clubs, a few leather strips, a random [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer"), and a [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") displayed on it. On the other side of the display is a [mammoth cheese bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl").

South of the display are a couple of drying racks with a bunch of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear") and two bunches of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam") hanging from them. A large mammoth cheese bowl is between the racks. East of the drying racks and past the path to the south are another two racks. Behind them is a tree, and behind that is a high ledge where two [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") can be found. Farther east from the racks is another rack with a bunch of dried elves ear and another mammoth cheese bowl nearby. Beyond this is a large rock formation, with a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") on a low ledge to the northeast. Beneath the rock is a pool of water fed by a wellspring. Submerged in front of the wellspring is a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), a [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and an apprentice-locked chest.

## Notes

- There is a high chance of the camp being attacked by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). If any survive the initial attack, they will flee toward [Orotheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Orotheim "Skyrim:Orotheim").
- Talking Stone Camp has more insect spawn points than any other location, with twenty-two total, allowing you to collect many [butterfly wings](/wiki/Skyrim:Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Butterfly Wing") and [blue butterfly wings](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly Wing") during the day and [luna moth wings](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth_Wing "Skyrim:Luna Moth Wing") and [torchbug thoraxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug_Thorax "Skyrim:Torchbug Thorax") at night. Twenty-three [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") plants also grow near the camp.
- A stream flowing east from the pool leads to a waterfall above an inlet to [River Hjaal](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Hjaal "Skyrim:River Hjaal"). Just above the waterfall is another iron ore vein. The corpse of an [alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemist "Skyrim:Alchemist") lies on an island in the middle of the inlet.
- A dirt path leading west from the campfire leads to a small stream. On the other side of the stream is another iron ore vein.

# Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Telvanni Tower.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Telvanni_Tower.png) | Settlement: Tel Mithryn ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Tel+Mithryn)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Tel_Mithryn "Lore:Tel Mithryn")) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2TelMithryn01, DLC2TelMithryn02 | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| East of [Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth") South-southeast of the [Sun Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Stone "Skyrim:Sun Stone") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Heart Stone Deposits](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") | 3 |

Tel Mithryn

**Tel Mithryn** is a Telvanni tower [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") east of [Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth") on [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim").

The settlement is home to [House Telvanni](/wiki/Lore:House_Telvanni "Lore:House Telvanni") Master Wizard [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth"). Its four mushroom structures were grown near the beginning of the [Fourth Era](/wiki/Lore:Fourth_Era "Lore:Fourth Era") out of special fungal spores from [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"). The structures include the [main tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)"), the [apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Apothecary "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Apothecary"), the [kitchen](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Kitchen "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Kitchen"), and the [steward's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Steward%27s_House "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Steward's House"). Master Neloth has a dubious reputation on the island, but is instrumental in progressing the *[Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")* questline and offers other [unique services](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_Enchanter "Skyrim:Staff Enchanter") to the enterprising adventurer.

Each of the structures is accessible by a long organic ramp ascending to a round wooden door. A [heart stone deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone_Deposit "Skyrim:Heart Stone Deposit") and a convenient [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") are behind the kitchen, with two more deposits on the cliffs near the coast to the southeast, while a few [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") and [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungi and [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") plants grow near the ramps. Other than the unique exterior architecture, most items of interest are inside the buildings.

## Tel Mithryn Residents

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

#### Dragonborn

- **[The Path of Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Path_of_Knowledge "Skyrim:The Path of Knowledge")**: Discover the locations of the Black Books in order to stop [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)").

#### Side Quests

- **[From the Ashes](/wiki/Skyrim:From_the_Ashes "Skyrim:From the Ashes")**: Help [Talvas Fathryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon") by killing an [ash guardian](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Guardian "Skyrim:Ash Guardian").
- **[Healing a House](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing_a_House "Skyrim:Healing a House")**: Help [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren") repair the tower of Tel Mithryn.
- **[Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward")**: Find a new steward for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

*The following quests become available after you've spoken to Neloth during Reluctant Steward.*

- **[Telvanni Research](/wiki/Skyrim:Telvanni_Research "Skyrim:Telvanni Research")**: Extract a sample from an [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth")'s research. *(Also requires Conjuration 40)*
- **[Heart Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stones "Skyrim:Heart Stones")**: Find a [heart stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").
- **[Experimental Subject (A)](/wiki/Skyrim:Experimental_Subject_(A) "Skyrim:Experimental Subject (A)")**: Help [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") by being a test subject in his experiment.
- **[Azra's Staffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Azra%27s_Staffs "Skyrim:Azra's Staffs")**: Retrieve a staff made by [Azra Nightwielder](/wiki/Lore:Azra_Nightwielder "Lore:Azra Nightwielder") for Master [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").

*The following quests become available after completing Reluctant Steward.*

- **[Black Book: The Hidden Twilight](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Hidden_Twilight_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Hidden Twilight (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Hidden_Twilight_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Hidden Twilight (book)")'s hidden knowledge.
- **[Briarheart Necropsy](/wiki/Skyrim:Briarheart_Necropsy "Skyrim:Briarheart Necropsy")**: Examine a [Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart") for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").

*The following quest becomes available after completing Experimental Subject (A) and requires [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") 40.*

- **[Wind and Sand](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_and_Sand_(quest) "Skyrim:Wind and Sand (quest)")**: Retrieve a copy of *[Wind and Sand](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_and_Sand_(book) "Skyrim:Wind and Sand (book)")* for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").

*The following quest becomes available after completing Briarheart Necropsy.*

- **[Old Friends](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Friends "Skyrim:Old Friends")**: Find the source of attacks on Tel Mithryn.

*The following quest becomes available after completing [The Gardener of Men](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gardener_of_Men "Skyrim:The Gardener of Men").*

- **[Lost Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knowledge "Skyrim:Lost Knowledge")**: Retrieve the [Black Books](/wiki/Lore:Black_Book "Lore:Black Book") for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").

#### Creation Club

- **[Ashen Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Heart "Skyrim:Ashen Heart")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Find out [who](/wiki/Skyrim:Erden_Relvel "Skyrim:Erden Relvel") attacked the temple and retrieve their [unique mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Dagoth_Ur "Skyrim:Mask of Dagoth Ur").
- **[Put A Fork In It](/wiki/Skyrim:Put_A_Fork_In_It "Skyrim:Put A Fork In It")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath"): Pass [Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath "Skyrim:Sheogorath")'s trial to earn his staff.
- **[The Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos"): Complete a mage's quest to reassemble two powerful staves.

## Notes

- The [Redoran Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard "Skyrim:Redoran Guard") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") seem to dislike this place, as they will occasionally say *"Headed east? May want to give Tel Mithryn a wide berth. I don't like the looks of that place one bit."*

Tel Mithryn Tower

**Tel Mithryn** is the main tower and home of [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") and his apprentice [Talvas Fathryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon") in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)").

It is by far the largest of the four mushroom structures in the settlement, between [Tel Mithryn Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Apothecary "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Apothecary") to the north and [Tel Mithryn Steward's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Steward%27s_House "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Steward's House") to the west.
