| --- |
| [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") [Spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Spells") [Trainer (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Master)")[Enchanting (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Enchanting (Master)")  [Talvas Fathryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon") [Spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Spells") [Trainer (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Master)")[Conjuration (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Conjuration (Master)") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") |

## Related Quests

:   *See [Tel Mithryn (settlement)](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)")*

## Tel Mithryn (tower)

The levitation shaft

The staff enchanter room

The entrance leads into the bottom of an enchanted vertical shaft, which allows you to float up and down between the entrance and the living quarters above. It is possible to fall and die from the upper area if the levitation activator is not used; [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") should be asked to remain outside for this reason (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

The levitation shaft is in the middle of the circular main chamber, with a railing around the edge. The chamber features many tables, sets of shelves, and crates holding a wide variety of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and [scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls"). The scattered ingredients include seven samples of [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), as Neloth enjoys canis root tea, brewed by his steward. Against the railing next to the arrival point is a table holding large smeltable Dwemer items like [solid Dwemer metal](/wiki/Skyrim:Solid_Dwemer_Metal "Skyrim:Solid Dwemer Metal"), with a second table holding similar Dwemer items nearby to the southeast. Farther to the southeast are two tables covered with maps of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") and [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim"), respectively. To the northeast is a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), an owned bedroll, and a few bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"). To the northwest are two [arcane enchanters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") set into two of the tables. Four [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") and one [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungi grow near the outer wall among the tables and crates to the northwest and southwest.

To the south is a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_Enchanter_Key "Skyrim:Staff Enchanter Key")-locked round door, beyond which is Neloth's [staff enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_Enchanter "Skyrim:Staff Enchanter"), a third arcane enchanter, and the *[Black Book: The Hidden Twilight](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Hidden_Twilight_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Hidden Twilight (book)")*. The key is obtained from Neloth after completing the quest [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward"). It is possible to buy [unenchanted staves](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves#Unenchanted_Staves "Skyrim:Staves") from Neloth and create your own staves using [heart stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") at the staff enchanter. To the east is a storeroom containing another chest, several sacks, some empty and unusable barrels, and more crates. To the north is a bedroom containing a single owned bed and more scattered full and empty wine bottles. To the west is the withered part of the tower, which will be replaced by a small prison holding two [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") after completing the quest [Healing a House](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing_a_House "Skyrim:Healing a House").

## Notes

- After completing the quest [Telvanni Research](/wiki/Skyrim:Telvanni_Research "Skyrim:Telvanni Research"), a number of potions and scrolls in the tower become unowned and free to take.
- If you commit a crime and Neloth becomes hostile, you may have difficulty escaping the tower, as the levitation trigger will become inactive.
- This location is also known as "Tel Mithryn Tower", one of the potential locations mentioned in the [*Scribbles of a Madman*](/wiki/Skyrim:Scribbles_of_a_Madman "Skyrim:Scribbles of a Madman").

## Bugs

- If a follower follows you into the tower, it's possible they will not exit with you when you leave. If you reenter the tower, and the follower wasn't tagged [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs"), you may find them dead on the upper or lower platforms. This is most likely caused by their inability to interact with the tower's levitation shaft, causing them to fall and die. This can be avoided by asking them to wait outside before you enter.
- Although Neloth tells you he will reserve a bed and a chest for your use after completing the quest [Old Friends](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Friends "Skyrim:Old Friends"), there will still be no chest clearly reserved for your use, and the bed in the steward's house will remain the only unowned bed or bedroll in the settlement.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.3, fixes this bug.
- The tower's local map shows two exits, but there is actually only one.
- The locked door can sometimes disappear, giving you free access to the black book and staff enchanter before completing the quest to obtain the key for the door. **?**
- It's possible, due to the tower's layout, for both Talvas and Neloth to fall down the shaft during their normal schedule. Normally, they will use the levitation mechanism to float back to the upper level, but if this happens to Neloth during the beginning of Old Friends (before he divines where Illdari is), he won't levitate himself back to the top and the quest will be stuck, requiring you to reload a save from before it happened. **?**
- The door to Neloth's staff enchanter blocks navigation when open, which can lead to some of his quests failing to run because he won't leave the room. The collision on the mesh apparently cuts the navmesh when it shouldn't.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. The door mesh has been modified so both halves will pull up into the ceiling to avoid this.
- Incomplete and/or broken mavmeshes can fail to prevent NPCs from walking off the edge of the platform where the "elevator" is.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.5, fixes this bug.

Tel Mithryn Apothecary

**Tel Mithryn Apothecary** is the home of the apothecary [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren") in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)").

It is one of the four mushroom structures in the settlement, north of [Tel Mithryn's tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)").

## Residents

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | Residents | | --- | | **[Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren")** [Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Apothecary") | |

## Related Quests

- **[Healing a House](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing_a_House "Skyrim:Healing a House")**: Help [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren") repair the tower of [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)").
- **[Hunting and Gathering](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_and_Gathering "Skyrim:Hunting and Gathering")**: Collect a rare alchemy [ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") for [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren").

## Tel Mithryn Apothecary

Tel Mithryn Apothecary interior

Elynea Mothren will sell apothecary supplies between 8am to 8pm. At other times, the entrance will be novice-locked.

The entrance leads into a small circular room comprising the entire interior. To the east is a table with a built-in [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") holding a [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"), six samples of [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"), a [potion of plentiful stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Stamina"), two [potions of ultimate magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Ultimate_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Ultimate Magicka"), a [paralysis poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralysis_Poison "Skyrim:Paralysis Poison"), a [draught of resist shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Resist_Shock "Skyrim:Draught of Resist Shock"), a sample of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), and a sample of [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), with two [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") and a [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") growing on the floor around the table. To the south is an open box containing two samples of bleeding crown, a sample of fly amanita, a sample of [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), a sample of Namira's rot, and a sample of white cap, a crate with a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") on top, a set of shelves with a potion of ultimate magicka on the floor in front of the shelves, a chair, and a white cap growing on the floor. The set of shelves holds a crate, a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), three [enchanter's philters](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanter%27s_Philter "Skyrim:Enchanter's Philter"), a [weak frenzy poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Frenzy_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Frenzy Poison"), three potions of plentiful stamina, a [potion of vigorous magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigorous_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Vigorous Magicka"), three paralysis poisons, a bowl of [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"), a sample of [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), a [swamp fungal pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod"), a sample of scaly pholiota, and two draughts of resist shock. To the west is a fly amanita growing on the floor next to a stack of crates, an owned single bed, and two [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle") and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on the floor around the bed.

## Notes

- After completing the quest [Healing a House](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing_a_House "Skyrim:Healing a House"), all low-value items in the building become unowned and free to take.
